# 太上三洞神咒

**The Supreme Three Caverns Divine Incantations**

**Sutra Title:** *The Supreme Three Caverns Divine Incantations*
**Author:** Unknown
**Volume:** Twelve
**Source Text:** *Daoist Canon of the Zhengtong Era*, Cavern of Perfection Section, Category of Original Texts

---

### *The Supreme Three Caverns Divine Incantations, Volume One*
**Incantations for Invoking Thunder, Prayers, and Commanding Spirits**

#### **Golden Light Divine Incantation**
The mysterious origin of Heaven and Earth,
Root of the ten thousand qi.
Through eons of cultivation,
My divine powers are realized.
Within and beyond the Three Realms,
I alone am revered.
My body radiates golden light,
Enveloping my form.
Invisible to sight, inaudible to sound,
It embraces Heaven and Earth,
Nurturing all living beings.
Recite it ten thousand times,
And my body shall shine with light.
The Three Realms shall guard me,
The Five Emperors shall attend.
Ten thousand spirits shall pay homage,
Thunder shall be commanded.
Demons and specters shall perish,
Evil spirits shall lose their form.
Within, the thunderclap resounds,
The Thunder Gods conceal their names.
*Ti-□ geng-□, □-□ lin-gu,*
*Hum bo ji li, xu heng □ bi,*
*□-□ duo jie, □-□ xi fu,*
*Yan zun □-□, □ hu □ chi, duo luo □-□.*
Wisdom and insight interpenetrate,
The five qi surge and soar.
Golden light swiftly manifests,
Shielding the Perfected One.

#### **Great Golden Light Divine Incantation**
Vast and boundless chaos,
The primordial qi first divided.
The golden light of true qi,
Is called the Jade Purity.
The Primordial Beginning fixed the forms,
Naturally supreme.
Blue and white rays intersect,
Establishing the Supreme Purity.
Within the Seven Treasures Palace,
The Jade Emperor of the Dao.
The three qi transform and coalesce,
Illuminating the Grand Purity.
Auspicious clouds grace the sacred halls,
The Five Spirits and Venerable Lord.
The central yellow qi,
Gives birth to the Jade Emperor.
Lord of the Six Desire Heavens,
Heavenly Lord of Brahma-qi.
Cinnabar clouds and azure vaults,
The Thunder Ancestor possesses spirit.
Within and beyond the Three Realms,
Ten thousand sages and thousand perfected.
Thirty-two Emperors,
Spirits of the Four Palaces and ten thousand numina.
Five Elders of the Five Directions,
Sun and Moon in grand harmony.
Radiant light intermingles,
Establishing Heaven and Earth.
Pure qi ascends,
Turbid qi descends and congeals.
Wondrous workings of the Eight Seas,
Water Emperor and Stream Perfected.
The Three Powers and Four Symbols,
Yin and Yang unite in form.
Nine ramparts of Fengdu,
Thunder conceals its name.
Hidden melodies of the heavens,
The Five Emperors oversee life.
Ten Blessings and Great Unity,
The Big Dipper governs the cosmos.
Green Emperor of Mount Zhong,
Myriad forms arrayed in splendor.
Spirit Lords *he-he*,
Essence of the Four-Eyed.
*Li heng wa li*, primordial true harmony.
The Emperor of Release conceals his chant,
The Dark and Mysterious One bows in reverence.
The Great Possession’s Jade Script,
Thunder roars mightily.
*Bo luo □ luo*, eternal life preserved.

#### **Assembly of Spirits Incantation**
Primordial Great Perfected,
Exalted Five Thunder Lords.
Radiant splendor of Mount Taihua,
Cavern Lord of the Eight Gates.
The Five Elders deliver decrees,
No hidden place goes unheard.
Above, they govern the Nine Heavens,
At the center, they restrain Mount Feng.
Below, they pacify rivers and seas,
Twelve eternal sources.
Eight Mighty Spirits devour,
Divine strategies and jade texts.
Summon dragons to bring rain,
Gather qi and condense mist.
Sun, Moon, and Five Planets,
The Seven Stars of the Big Dipper.
The United Brightness Heavenly Emperor,
Commands the Supreme Mystery.
Proclaim might through the Three Realms,
No delay shall be tolerated.
All heavens, all earths,
All waters, all mountains.
The jade perfected’s retinue,
Vast and profound great spirits.
Immortal Kings feast and wander,
Great Marshals bear banners.
Heavenly Soldiers march forth,
Golden Tigers charge behind.
Fierce beasts of the heavens,
Guard the four gates.
What is called arrives instantly,
What is summoned appears before me.
The Red Script blazes forth,
Wind and fire without pause.
Registers respond to commands,
Golden horses relay decrees.

#### **Great Thunder Divine Incantation of Mighty Virtue**
*Om hum hum,*
Three *dana*, Han Nan Yan Qian She Chi,
Arise, Nine Heavens Capital Fire Thunder Division,
Unbounded Mighty Spirit Kings:
Nine Heavens Fire Thunder, Fire Lightning, Fire Flight, Fire Rush, Fire Flow, Fire Seven Stars, Fire Thunderclap, Fire Flame Thunder, and Fierce Fire.
The Nine Heavens Capital Fire Thunder King is stern,
Riding leviathan dragons, mounted on flying tigers, lions, Bai Ze, Xiezhi, qilin, fire camels, fire elephants, fire horses, fire eagles, and ten thousand fire beasts.
Copper-headed, iron-faced, a million divine soldiers,
Five Emperors’ ritual axes,
Patrolling the Four Heavens.
The Emperor’s bell resounds,
Demons and ghosts all tremble.
Grotto heavens and blessed lands,
Mountains and rivers’ hidden spirits.

Mountains collapse and trees sink,
A hundred valleys boil and surge.
What spirit dares resist?
Those who do not submit shall be compelled.

The Wind King with his gaping maw,
Fire dragons and fire horses,
Fire lads and fire maidens,
Descend from Heaven—*bing* and *ding* surge forth.
Fire tigers spread their *qi*,
Eight dragons race and soar.
The Five Generals of the Capital Heaven,
Devouring thunder, roar aloud,
Sending sand flying and stones rolling,
Uprooting trees and displacing roots.
Wind chariots press from the left,
Fire chariots advance from the right.
Illuminating the Three Realms,
Transforming into a crimson city.
Beneath the Dipper’s base, the Eight Trigrams array,
Encompassing all four directions.
Might blankets the world,
Fierce and blazing, its power soars.
When ghostly spirits behold it,
They plunge ten thousand fathoms into the earth,
Reduced to flying ash.
Ancient trees and malevolent shrines,
For aeons lost in dust and confusion.

**Swift as the command of the Primordial Lady of Great Unity!**

---

**Divine Incantation of the Lesser Wood Lad of the Three Mountains of Great Unity**
Radiant *qian*-crystal gleams east of the Jade Pool,
The Alliance’s mighty envoy, named Azure Youth.
Hurl fire a thousand miles into the *kan* and *zhen* palaces,
Brave riders swiftly advance, coming to Great Meng.
The Wood Lad, mighty hero of the Three Mountains of Great Unity,
Thunderclaps shatter stone, spring sources flow free.
From *kun* to *xun*, the gates of the Luminous Elder,
Four fierce steeds charge with rushing fire.
Flowing essence and dense radiance race toward Zhurong,
The great spirit of Mount Taihua ascends amid clouds.
Black banners and dark silkworm standards wave in the void,
Obscuring the sun, steaming the rain, clouds mass thick.
Yanbo shakes the peaks of Kunlun,
Hidden spirits churn the seas, uniting with Dark Obscurity.
Feng Yi drums and dances, howling winds arise,
Penglai’s weak waters stir the merit of Xudu.
Dragons and eagles, swift and keen, first repel misfortune,
Crimson-haired, vast-winged, with eyes of flame.
Thunder and lightning spew venom, driving the Five Dragons,
The Four Seas shrouded in gloom, enmeshing yin’s forms.
At one cry, the Four Seas darken,
Where rain formations pass, rivers surge in flood.
Golden light streams, severing drought’s rainbows,
Summoning the hidden spirits of Yang Grottoes.
The Jade Thunder’s luminous master transforms Kongtong,
The Void Emperor of Mount Taihua sweeps away demonic flames.
The Dark Radiance of the Multitude, heralded as vanguard,
Shrine springs rage like clams, overawing Heaven’s Lord.
Rushing fire commands overturn the vault of heaven,
Whips strike demonic sprites, driving snakes and insects.
Goulou and Jili blaze with scorching traces,
Dengseng and Zeze all heed and obey.
The Four Singing Maidens, loyal at heart,
Assist me in relieving drought—merit resplendent.
Red cockerels and purple geese soar without end,
Seizing malevolence, binding evil, dispatching them to Northern Feng.
By decree of the Purple Void Primordial Lady, descend and seize!

**Swift as the command of the Great Marshal of the Fire Bell!**

---

**Divine Incantation of the Great Wood Lad**
*Qian*-essence streams radiance east of the Jade Pool,
The Alliance’s sagely envoy, named Azure Youth.
Hurl fire a thousand miles into the *kan* and *zhen* palaces,
Brave riders swiftly advance, coming to Great Meng.
When Chaos was split open, piercing Kongtong,
Green waves bore the heavens, turning toward Gou Rong.
The Azure Flower’s secret decree commands the sealing,
Overseeing talismanic orders, descending to the imperial palace.
The Wood Lad, mighty hero of the Three Mountains of Great Unity,
Reverently upholds the Mysterious Subtle, following with utmost devotion.
With a rush, he drives thunder, rousing sleeping dragons,
Thunderclaps shatter stone, spring sources flow free.
From *kun* to *xun*, the gates of the Luminous Elder,
Flowing essence and dense radiance race toward Zhurong.
Four fierce steeds charge with rushing fire,
Mighty mounts ascend Mount Taihua amid clouds.
Golden hammers and jade iron gleam with fire bows,
Startling heaven’s drums resound *dong-dong*.
The Heavenly Stem Great Sage descends with true wisdom,
The Divine Empyrean’s talismanic orders shine with numinous power.
Striking ten thousand evils, leaving no trace,
I now, by command, summon the Thunder Duke.
East, west, south, north—rushing fire throngs,
Banners and pennants flutter in the void by day.
Asuras, barred for a day, return to Sang Yong,
The Vaisravana envoy, Tian Yuan Yong.
The Kun’s tail sways, heaven’s vault trembles,
The Flame Emperor steams the rain, clouds mass thick.
In an instant, the *kan* position swells with black *qi*,
The Void Star blazes fiercely, piercing both pupils.
Yanbo shakes the peaks of Kunlun,
Driving thunder and lightning, straddling fire dragons.
Sand flies, stones roll, soaring through the void,
Hidden spirits churn the seas, uniting with Dark Obscurity.
Feng Yi drums and dances, howling winds arise,
The Four Singing Maidens, heralded as vanguard.
Goulou and Jili drive the Azure Dragon,
*Ding* and *xin* drip of old, grasping the Emperor’s bell.
The Alliance’s mighty envoy, frost congeals in winter,
The Jade Light Lad pounds the long spring pestle.
Mute mouths spew fury, roaring through the vault of heaven,
Dull brightness fades, venomous centipedes burned.
Huang Li wields his sword, slaying *chi* and serpents,
Han ministers, by command, inspect your forms.
Penglai’s weak waters stir the merit of Xudu,
The immortal retinue of Yingzhou returns with jade chimes.
When the Jade Treasury’s orders descend, none dare idle,
A hundred bureaus proffer decrees, all obey without fail.
Heavenly thunder rumbles, clashing with golden bells,
Divine thunder’s might shatters the canopy of Meng.
Dragon thunder shakes, heaven’s fire burns red,
Water thunder drums waves, seas swell full.
Earth spirits strike, smiting demonic throngs,
The *li*-yang drought demons vanish without trace.
Cornered Kang’s long bows sweep away rainbows,
Six-One, swift and keen, first repels misfortune.
Crimson-haired, vast-winged, with eyes of flame,
Thunder and lightning spew venom, driving the Five Dragons.
The Four Seas shrouded in gloom, enmeshing yin’s weight,
Follow my Yu step, descending with numinous power.
Heaven and earth tremble at the resounding crash,
Severing the drought spirits and all demonic lineages.
Firelight scatters, ten thousand miles burn red,
Burning away all evil, leaving no dust behind.
At the talisman’s arrival, rain flows freely,
Thunder and lightning arise, drums resound *dong-dong*.
Driving the thunder hosts, black rain follows,
At one cry, the Four Seas darken.
Golden radiance fills the marsh, flying in solemn harmony,
*Kan* initiates, *li* orders, commanding the Mysterious Lineage.
Water patterns hasten change, Heaven’s Gate appears,
Lightning flashes through the void, flames sear.
Gongbin wields his halberd, descending with Gonggong,
Where rain formations pass, rivers surge in flood.
Thunderclaps shake the seas in great circles,
The Lord of Brightness, Primordial Emperor, heralded as vanguard.
Shangyang calls, cloud-coiffed and loose,
Red cockerels and purple geese overturn golden cages.
Flowing cinnabar and auspicious *qi* rise in luxuriant profusion,
The Ninefold Heaven’s Gate hangs with crimson maples.
The Old Man of Mount Tai meets Feng Meng,
The Numinous Lord of Mount Heng commands Red Pine.
The Western Flower’s Metal Heaven employs the Four Fiends,
Mount Heng’s Black Pottery startles Yu’s offerings.
The Central Amalgamation of the Five Luminaries faces Heaven’s Song,
A hundred spirits descend from the void, driving with divine wisdom.
*Du zhe*, *jiu luo*, slay flying insects,
Ice doves warm the stone caves of A Xiong.
Holding the jade tablet, extending years, the steadfast Bear,
Wu Meng and Huang Xing, Zhao’s traces revealed.
Rong Xiong and Gui Yan flash like *jiu* and *peng*,
Si Quan and Zi Zhen awe Heaven’s Lord.

**Swift as the command of the Fire Bell’s Great Marshal!**

The Two Patriarchs of Dongyuan return to embrace the Emperor,
Envoys bearing staffs traverse the sky with transverse flutes.
Heavenly demons block the Dao, yet none dare attack,
The Hibiscus-lined Brocade River sings of Kongtong.

The Divine Empyrean scrutinizes human joys and sorrows,
The Jade Tablet commands the hosts of thunder gods.
Beheading tigers and leopards, slaying fierce gibbons,
Countless generals and officials fret with anxious hearts.

With single-minded devotion, they bow and revere the Jade Countenance,
The hosts of heaven and constellations align without disorder.
All phenomena belong to the Mysterious Mechanism’s lineage,
Water-bearing envoys come and go amidst them.

Heaven’s grace descends in long, flowing streams,
Aiding my Dao and its law to flourish daily.
Aiding me to rescue from drought and transform the times into abundance,
Aiding me to rescue from drought—meritorious deeds resplendent.

All myriad evils and slaughters are eradicated without trace,
All things attain completion and return to the Great Kiln.
Heaven’s glory is shared, its merit boundless.

**The Purple Sovereign of the Southern Culmen, Primordial Lord, descends by decree.**
**Swift as the Fire Bell’s command, seize and execute!**

---

**Fourfold Spirit Incantation**
Protect the Radiant Primordial Consort, Pure Flower of Gold,
The Celestial Heroes of the Dipper’s Handle and the Mysterious Numinous.
The Primordial Lady of the Great Monad commands the water soldiers,
The Penglai Envoys marshal the thunderous waters.

The Weak River gleams pellucid, free of the slightest impurity,
Gathering all river sources into the Four Directions.
The gods of the Four Seas are the essence of Heaven’s Monad,
Driving chariots and conveying water to open Heaven’s City.

The Nine Abysses of the Great Yin’s frigid waters,
Within them dwell the cavernous yang spirits of the Dark and Mysterious.
The Jade Thunder’s luminous masters swiftly raise their voices,
Mighty steeds bearing the Great Flower of Heaven race ahead.

Flowing essences and dense radiance rush toward the Fire Bells,
Black clouds billow as the sea’s *qi* ascends.
Rain pours down upon the hundred rivers like a flood,
Moistening the land inch by inch until all is full and brimming.

The Rain Masters and their subordinates, the stars Rahu and Ketu,
Receive their orders and swiftly reach the stars Ji and Bi.
Fish-dragons soar across the sky, their fins and scales stirring,
Waves and breakers surge as the great whale surges forth.

The brocade-scaled creatures’ every pore pours forth the hundred rivers,
The Red Talismans lie hidden, their luminous time surging.
The Supreme Emperor’s decree brooks no delay,
A Xiang scatters flowers, bearing Heaven’s fragrance.

Swiftly command the envoys to uphold the statutes,
Strike open the lapis lazuli vase with the jade staff,
Let the rain’s essence pour forth to nourish all living things.

**By the Fire Bell General’s authority, in accordance with the Supreme Emperor’s decree!**
The Jade Clarity commands me with the Nine Heavenly Numinous Chapters,
Clouds fly to eradicate calamities and misfortunes.
The Thirty-Six Envoys and the Four Seas’ Wooden Lords of the Three Mountains,
By the yang power of the sun, seize and execute!

---

**Great Cavern—One Hundred Great Auspicious Incantation of the Resonant Harmonious Luminous Jade Sound**
The Incantation of the One Hundred Great Auspicious Resonant Harmonious Luminous Jade Sound of the Primordial Beginning’s Skillful and Kindly Pure Harmony, Opening the Gateway of the True Dharma:

Universal Light, Vast Salvation, Revered One,
The True Unity of the Great Mystery’s heart.
The Great Cavern’s cinnabar abyss strikes,
The pure harmony of auspicious sounds.

Beginning, beginning, beginning—threefold *qi*,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Brahma sound of the great Brahma *qi*,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The Heavenly sound of pure and wondrous tones,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Emperor’s heart in samadhi’s sound,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The Jade sound of fragrant and radiant hues,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The void’s sound of the Dao’s luminous masters,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The soundless sound of wondrous and mysterious penetration,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Dao’s Ancestor’s inner sound proclaimed,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the Primordial Lord of the Great Monad,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Supreme Emperor’s sound of wondrous conduct,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The golden sound of unequaled tones,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the Nine Numinous Jade Mother,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The Eastern Father’s divine sound of splendor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Yi sound of the Dongyuan Revered One,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The abyssal sound of the cavern’s numinous sorrow,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The fragrant sound of the cavern’s emptiness,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The wheel’s sound of the great dragon’s radiance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The wind’s sound of the Eight Harmonies’ spirits,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The wing’s sound of the cavern’s contemplative splendor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The lamp’s sound of the cavern’s illumination,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the Heavenly Emperor dispelling obstructions,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The water’s sound of the cavern’s mystery,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The incense of the Empyrean’s radiant Flower of Heaven,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The fruit’s sound of the cavern’s subtlety,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sprout’s sound of the cavern’s numen,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The abyssal strike of the central sound,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The golden nectar’s flow from the cavern’s source,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The jade and rose-gem’s mysterious breast’s savor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of golden rice’s lament,
The Yellow Primordial Grain of the cavern’s void.
The purple treasure’s meal of the Eight Harmonies,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The black sound of the great bright wheel,
The inexhaustible resources of the cavern’s purity.
The black pearl’s auspicious radiance averts misfortune,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The mother’s sound of the primordial vessel,
The Heavenly Emperor’s raiment of the cavern’s truth.
The yellow skirt of purple radiance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The Golden Mother’s sound of the pivot and hinge,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The lotus boat’s sound of the vast and luminous,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The skirt’s sound of purple radiance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the great perfect penetration,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the wondrous heavenly flowers,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the soaring Black Dragon,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the great true suchness,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the precious moon’s pure and august,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the towering sun’s wisdom and radiance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the crystal net’s strength,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the Taiyuan’s song poured forth,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the compassionate father’s chapter,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The sound of the stars and constellations’ morning emperor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the carved rose’s wondrous fragrance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The fragrance of the thoroughwort and rose of the Great Mystery,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The inner fragrance of the Central Emperor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The pure scene’s jade and august fragrance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The true fragrance of the cavern’s spirits,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The divine sound of the Great Clarity’s hymn,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The wondrous gate’s true and settled fragrance,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The *qi*-mother’s fragrance of trailing splendor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sagely sound of the Heavenly Treasure Emperor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The true emperor’s sound of the numinous born,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The immortal king’s sound of the divine treasure,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The master’s treasure of the mysterious center’s sound,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

The song’s cycle completes the Great Clarity,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The incantation’s sound of dawning sunlight,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The swift sound of jade’s cooling splendor,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The elephant’s sound of supreme virtue,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The first sound of great felicity,
The emperor’s heart, resonant, harmonious.
The dark and still sound of the mysterious passage,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The profound sound of the Lofty Observing King,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The responsive sound of Southern Longevity,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The pure and harmonious sound of wondrous transformation,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The haughty sound of the Eight Florals,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The blessed sound of the Longevity Immortal King,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of the Primal Clear Emperor’s charge,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The subduing sound of the Cloud-Elder’s beginning,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The flowing chant of A-Yi’s melody,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The lush and flourishing sound of nurturing growth,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The answering sound of great Brahma’s joy,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The luminous sound of the returning mystery,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The resonant call of Yu-Yuan and Dragon-Net,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The cavern’s floating sound of jade’s life,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The empty and numinous sound of Ze-Luo’s choice,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The green silk’s sound of cloud-borne flight,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The nurturing sound of Na-Yu and Mara,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The mirror’s sound of fate’s unfolding visage,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The vast and radiant sound of the divine tassel,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The meditative sound of the White Prime’s plan,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The spreading sound of Po-Ni’s grace,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Brahma-sprout’s sound of misty seclusion,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The boundless sound of the distant and infinite,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The lush and flourishing sound of Yu-Zhu’s beginning,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The extending sound of Yan-You’s self-debate,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The ranked sound of the canopy’s support,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of Chang-Sang’s cypress in emptiness,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The simian’s sound of the Upper Mystery’s nurture,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of Tuo-Luo’s cloud-gathering,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The flying sound of the heavenly sand,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The radiant and fresh sound of harmony’s center,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The azure vault’s sound of Floating Li,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The sound of preserving truth and dispelling darkness,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The cavern’s wondrous sound of vast expanse,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The human heart’s sound of Ze-Na’s choice,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.
The Great Cavern’s boundless sound,
Auspicious, resonant, harmonious.

Three thousand perfections of the mysterious work,
Eight hundred wonders of the wondrous practice align.
Noble ranks birth the mushroom’s bloom,
Cinnabar and azure glow with the numinous treasure’s light.
Perfect fulfillment attains the ten penetrations,
The form ascends to the Three Subtleties.

The Most High Cavern Abyss Samadhi,
Great Sage of Peng and Lin,
Compassionate and unobstructed,
Majestic virtue vast and profound,
Pervading the ten directions,
Governing the three realms,
Radiant seal of stillness,
The emperor’s heart subdues demons,
Saves and protects all beings,
Dispels disasters and erases sins,
Unravels karmic knots and dissolves bonds,
The Great Auspicious Dhāraṇī Chapter.

Invocation:
We reverently invoke the Unobstructed Master of the Cavern Abyss,
Primordial Emperor of the Void before kalpas,
Supreme Honored One.
Expounding the samadhi of divine incantations,
Transmitting the Way to the myriad Dao’s ancestors.
The Cavern Abyss Heavenly Worthy of Great Majesty,
Once vowed to aid all heavens.
Twenty-two vows to save all beings,
Broadly enabling the severance of demonic lineages.
Thousands of karmic grievances and myriad sins all dissolved,
Nine calamities and three disasters wholly swept away.
Clearly and firmly, beings attain liberation,
All ascend together to the supreme Dao.
Whatever is sought through single-minded devotion,
All shall achieve, aligning with mortal hearts.
Subduing the six great demon kings of the caverns,
Restraining the six yin’s ghostly thieves.
Unraveling karmic knots with the pure harmony’s method,
Dispersing misfortune and ending disputes with the auspicious sound.
Unrelenting and unabandoning, great compassion,
Virtues like a wondrous forest, impossible to exhaust.
Your servant now proclaims the Emperor’s Heart Incantation,
To save and protect all beings, guiding those with karmic affinity.
The emperors of the ten directions and three realms,
The eight divisions of dragons and spirits, the earth deities,
Those who listen to the scripture and guard the Dharma,
Whether on earth or in the empty sky.
At the first hearing of the divine incantation, the emperor’s bell sways,
Each assumes their majestic bearing to offer protection.

The Great Cavern’s encompassing might,

rain does not fall.

do not delay!

heaven and earth, sun and moon,

Swift retribution be!

**Star Marshal Incantation**
Great One Star Marshal,
his name shakes the Nine Heavens.
Receiving the thunderous decree,
his transformations arise naturally.
Roaring winds and rains,
mountains, stones, rivers, and floods.
His body sways and dances,
flying dragons course through heaven.
Great Hua trembles,
thunder resounds through the skies.
Rahu and Ketu clash,
water and fire surge wildly.
Comets and meteors charge boldly,
metal and fire soar on all sides.
Wood and Earth create and transform—
the decree issues from the mysterious and profound!
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Great Yang Star Marshal**
Holding authority, he supports Fusang,
his solar wheel spans ten thousand leagues,
glorious in the eastern quarter.
True talismans take flight,
scattering firelight everywhere.

**Wood Star’s Annual Splendor**
Presiding over the eastern direction,
startled insects stir in the Thunder Chamber.
True talismans take flight—
thunder’s might grows strong.

**Mars Enforces the Law**
Sternly driving his swift steeds,
wielding authority over the Three Realms—
ghosts and spirits tremble in fear.
True talismans take flight—
fiery flames fly swiftly.

**Venus Traverses the Han**
Wandering the Eight Seas,
its radiant spirit scatters brilliance,
awakening the blades of war.
True talismans take flight—
demonic essences perish.

**Water’s Virtue Awaits Dawn**
Governing the spirits of water,
the Three Rivers and Nine Streams,
lakes, seas, and dragon deities.
True talismans take flight—
floodwaves surge in all directions.

**Central Earthly Host**
Governing qi’s Yellow Prime,
the Thearch’s decreed ranks,
the Four Symbols complete.
True talismans take flight—
earth quakes and mountains shift.

**Divine Head, Rahu**
Pushed forward by the Five Thearchs,
one glare of its enraged eyes—
mountains and peaks collapse.
True talismans take flight—
earth’s qi swiftly ascends.

**Divine Tail, Ketu**
Black qi shakes the heavens,
dimming the sun and obscuring the moon—
none dare face its divine might.
True talismans take flight—
thunder and rain follow in its wake.

**Celestial One’s Purple Qi**
Dao’s radiant honor,
dissolving clashes and dispelling evil,
transforming misfortune and averting calamity.
True talismans take flight—
great rites proceed.

**Comet and Meteor**
Divine valor and might,
one roar to the south—
its voice shakes thunder.
True talismans take flight—
stones split and mountains topple.

**Green Yang’s Mercy**
Examiner of decrees,
transmitting talismans to resolve the Ten Spirits.
True talismans descend—
fury swiftly ceases.
None dare defy—
obey the decree and act!
Nine Heavens’ Thearch,
issue the command and act.
I wield the true talisman,
charging through the stars.
Rebellious currents clash and shift—
slaying qi swirls in chaos.
The decree is transmitted—
each star returns to its station.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Flying Dipper Spirit Incantation**
Supreme Great Clarity,
Mysterious Origin Thearch.
Protect life and guard destiny,
decreeing the capture of the Three Hun.
Spirit talismans guard the Po—
ghosts and spirits stand revealed.
Command me to approach the palace,
crossing the mysterious gate.
Ascend the Jade Court,
facing the exalted perfected.
Come and go with clarity,
reverently presenting my sincerity—
the Jade Thearch’s decree!
Swiftly obey!

**Five Spirit Talisman Ingestion Incantation**
Jade Mansion’s Mysterious Palace,
purple qi’s beginning in green.
Within, refine the Three Hun—
the Terrace of Light is peaceful.
Spirit treasures of the Jade Chamber,
born with me.
Do not move recklessly—
the Yellow Court’s supervising spirit.
Great Numen guards and protects.
Should you wish to fly,
your form ascends to Jade Clarity.
Hungry or thirsty—
swallow and drink jade essence!
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Flying Spirit Incantation**
Heaven bright, qi clear,
Three Lights perfectly luminous.
Golden chambers, jade rooms—
Five Sacred Fungi flourish.

illuminating my form.

**The Great Highest’s Three Caverns Divine Incantations, Scroll Two Concluded**

**The Great Highest’s Three Caverns Divine Incantations, Scroll Three**
*Incantations for Thunder, Prayers, Exorcisms, and Command*

---

**Yang Dipper Mantra**
Essential and wondrous, the twelve celestial hours—
ride the Heavenly Stem’s martial might arrayed.
Qi drifts and sways like floating clouds,
nine transformations stir, ascending to Heaven’s accord.
Know change and fix fortune’s weal or woe,
contract the vast, discern its bounds.
Pass through the Dipper’s lodges, traverse Heaven’s Gate,
join the Six Pitches, grasp Jia and Yi’s hold.
Tread Heaven’s Glory, mount Heaven’s Task,
clear and deep the abyss—walk the land as though sunk.
Beside Heaven’s Pillar, embrace Heaven’s Heart,
thence cross over to ascend Heaven’s Bird.
Lean on Heaven’s Auxiliary, face Heaven’s Thrust,
enter Heaven’s Inner, exit Heaven’s Vast.
The Dipper’s Dao flows, hard and soft unite,
all blessings and fortunes stream to later ages.
Emerge from the dim and distant—thousands, ten thousands of years!

After one chant, pace the six hours,
nine chants, three steps—three hundred years.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

---

**Yin Dipper Mantra**
Sun and moon bright, Heaven and Earth paired,
the human Dao rises, the ghostly Dao decays.
I enter from Heaven’s Vast into Heaven’s Inner,
briefly pass Heaven’s Thrust, meet Auxiliary’s retreat.
Return to face Heaven’s Bird and the Heart,
grasp Heaven’s Pillar, convene with Glory and Task.
The Dipper’s steps traverse, guided by pure spirit—
the human Dao flows, the ghostly Dao obstructed,
a thousand evils, ten thousand impurities all retreat.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

---

**Summoning the Eastern Thunder Spirit Incantation**
Eastern Yang’s shaking spirit, Thunder and Lightning’s true honored one.
Call the wind, *ya-□*, command *Jiu Luo*’s truth.
Fanged and fierce officers, fire chariots, fire wheels.
Swiftly, Fire Elder Wen, thunderbolts charge ahead.
Mighty radiance roars, shaking Heaven and Earth.
Marshals and great generals, smash demons, subdue spirits.
Master of sun and rain, fell temples, behead spirits.
Ascend to Heaven, split the earth, awe the Dipper’s numen.
Shining spirit of Great Hua, sacred light’s wondrous power.
Four seas’ Yang cavern, descend to my altar.
The Three Clarities’ decree descends, Jade Pivot’s command enacted.
Five Peaks’ honored ones, shake mountains, drive the rain.
Overturn seas, race clouds—summon the marshal by talisman.
Primal Beginning’s Jade Measure, save and protect all beings,
descend at the Xun Gate.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Summoning the Southern Thunder Spirit Incantation**
Southern brilliance gleams, *Bing Jiu Luo*’s truth.
True essence of Yang spirit, warmth of the fiery lodge’s power.
Five Directions’ thunderbolts, Stone River’s mighty voice.
Thunder’s radiance transforms, the Nine Provinces’ altar commands.
Sacred light’s ferocity, great fire wheels spread.
Fire clouds ten thousand fathoms, eight chariots, eight wheels.
Thunderbolts charge ahead, High Heaven’s decree enacted.
All Heaven’s quaking thunder, Jade Dawn’s cavern power.
Water Department binds heads, fire demons’ forms destroyed.
Chunqiu’s true lord, Purple Void’s spirit communer.
Great general who fells evil, swiftly act!
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

Devour demons, consume spirits, fell evil, smash the perverse.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

Master of sun and rain, gather souls, collect spirits.
Penglai’s department, Wind and Rain’s high minister.

General of rosy lightning, smash demons, subdue spirits.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Summoning the Central Thunder Spirit Incantation**
Sacred spirit’s ferocity, shaking Heaven and Earth.

**Thunder Dispelling Prayer**

**Exorcising the Qian Toxin King**
The mighty Qian Toxin King, whose awe subdues the nether realms.
Eight Immortals wield halberds; the Five Spirits of the Highest command.
The Supreme Mystery descends in radiance; seven gods guard the court.
Yellow Perfected shines with talismans, brandishing fire bells in splendor.
Divine tigers roar and spew; venomous winds rage in chaos.
Purple Comet spans the Two Modes; Four Tassels gaze upward in clarity.
Primordial essence of the Nine Heavens, crystalline essence of the Four Skies.
Within, coiled with primordial qi; without, marshaled by generals and troops.
Left, they intimidate; right, they pacify—wind strikes, fire conquers.
With a shout, ten thousand demons are slain; a thousand spirits are beheaded.
When the Golden Perfected’s singular seal is invoked, evil demons vanish.
The Northern Feng collapses; all it destroys is overthrown.
I bear the true script—commanding the Five Spirits.
The Three Origins unite with the Perfected; Duke Qie aligns with the Emperor’s sincerity.
The Supreme Emperor of the Grand Tenuity ascends to the Three Pure Ones.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Southern Dipper Fire Bell Incantation**
Southern Dipper Fire Bell, Celestial Soldiers of the Highest.
Mighty warriors of the Nine Heavens, five hundred maidens-at-arms.
Heads crowned with celestial diadems, bodies aflame in crimson form.
I, with upright integrity, annihilate evil and purge spirits.
Four Great Gods roam, patrolling the city in majesty.
Eight Mighties wield venom; the Thousand-Eyed Venerable.
Expel a hundred specters; malevolent toxins shake heaven’s net and earth’s snare.
Seize and capture demonic spirits.
Hands grasp the killing cord; heads bear the Seven Stars.
Obscure sun and moon; shake the cosmos.
Illuminate heaven and earth; nimble clouds never cease.
Command the Earth Deities; register the myriad spirits.
Shatter the Five Peaks; topple Kunlun.
Eyes bulging, glaring—execute and behead demonic spirits.
Heavenly gods assist; thunder and lightning follow.
Entering earth, all is purified; entering water, the abyss clears.
Weapons disperse; blades vanish.
Burn mountains to ash; boil waters into scalding broth.
What spirit does not fear? What ghost dares stand before?
Three thousand Mars stars, eighty thousand fire calamities.
Gathered into the palace, scattered to the ends of the sky.
Giant flames ten thousand yards high, blazing inferno filling heaven.
In an instant, ten thousand miles—burning across the Three Thousand.
Seas parched dry; weapons reduced to fine dust.
The Highest’s decree—impartial law.
Molten gold becomes water; scorched iron turns to mud.
Douse you, demons—dare to face me?
The Highest’s edict—swiftly obey!
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Temple-Smiting Thunder Summons**
August Heaven births me; August Earth bears me.
August Heaven nurtures me; August Earth rears me.
My seal is in my hand; my incantation in my mouth.
Head crowned with the Celestial Stem; feet treading the Northern Dipper.
Wind Earl and Rain Master; Thunder Duke roars.
Smite temples, expel spirits—gods and ghosts flee in haste.
The might of thunderbolts; lightning follows.
Execute and annihilate gods and ghosts, reducing them to fine dust.
Demons, specters, and malevolent spirits—forever eradicated, roots severed.
I uphold the Emperor’s decree—demolishing the Ghost Gate.
Heaven and earth darken; sun and moon dim.
Spirits, demons, and thieves—none dare escape their form.
Hastily exterminate, sweeping away demonic miasma.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Sealing the Demon Temple Gate Incantation**
Southern Fire Decree, dispatching the Six Dings.
Mighty warriors of the Nine Heavens, a million spirit soldiers.
Seal springs—springs dry; seal stones—stones split.
Seal mountains—mountains crumble; seal rivers—rivers run dry.
Seal temples—temples shatter; seal fire—fire extinguishes.
Seal gods—gods perish; seal ghosts—ghosts are obliterated.
Decree of the Three Heavens—all are gathered and subdued.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Exorcism Incantation**
Vermilion Bird soars in radiance; divine might expands within.
Four Mountain Sources pacify; ghostly soldiers flee.

Uplifting mountains, cleaving heaven—divine birds and venomous dragons.

Spewing flames ten thousand yards, eradicating misfortune.
Legions of spirits, banished to mountain villages.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Prayer for Clear Skies**
Flying Heaven’s sudden fire, resplendent solar crystal.

**Mārīcī’s Minor Subjugation Mantra**
Namaḥ ratna-trayāya. Tadyathā: oṃ dhara dhara dhara-dhara-dhare āḷoḍa āḷoḍa garuḍa garuḍa sarva-buddha-bodhisattva-tri-mantra-padā māra-dhara dhara-dhare āḷi-pāḷi-pāḷi sarva-garuḍa āḷi-pāḷi yaya-kṣe bhiḥ svāhā. Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Oath of the Xin Heavenly Lord**
Thunderous and fierce divine officials, your might rules the Nine Celestial Courts.
Moving within the Three Realms, you loyally assist the Thearch-Lord.
Your body surges ten thousand fathoms tall, known as the honored ones of the Thunder Department.
You oversee all thunder bureaus, the Wind Earls and Rain Masters.
The mothers of lightning and thunderbolts, the mighty yakṣa hosts—
Left and right, you bear Heaven’s mandate, aiding the Five Thunder Lords.
I act by the Jade Emperor’s decree to save the people of the world.
Whoever upholds this shall see me manifest my form.
Summon me to the celestial realms, and I shall ascend to report to the Thearch-Lords.
Summon me to the netherworld, and I shall descend to the Palace of Shades.
Summon me to the watery palaces, and the four seas’ waves shall churn.
Summon me to the yang realms, and I shall instantly deliver all beings.
Summon me to seize demonic spirits, and I shall shatter their ghostly camps.
Summon me to command generals, and the generals shall swiftly awaken to spirit.
Summon me to attack the sick, and the sick shall at once find peace.
Summon me to deliver the dead, and the dead shall instantly ascend.
Be with me from beginning to end, together as ministers to the Jade Emperor.
Should you violate Heaven’s laws, nine generations shall suffer poisonous punishment.
Should I betray you, the sun and moon above shall dim.
Below, the springs shall dry, and no grass or tree shall grow.
Forever a ghost of the dark netherworld, never able to ascend to the Highest Clarity.
On the days of *rén* and *guǐ*, I descend—be diligent in upholding this.
Offer pure tea and jujube broth, burn peachwood incense.
I shall appear at your side—calm your heart, do not fear.
Together we make this great vow: to save all beings.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Oath of Envoy Zhang**
Disorderly Heaven’s envoy, swift and mighty in spirit.
Aiding the chief marshal, rousing thunder and subduing gods.
By this oath I set, burn hundred-fold incense in the censer.
Instantly descend to my left and right, enhancing my divine might.
Should you slight this oath, Heaven’s punishment shall strike your body.
Should you violate my precepts, you shall forever sink into the Sea of Delusion.
Receiving the Emperor’s command, you ride mists and raise clouds.
On *jiǎxū* days I descend—record your deeds and submit them.
Your nine generations shall be destroyed, never to prosper.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Oath of the Generals**
You are the essence of Heaven; I am the spirit of Earth.
I divide your essence and merge it with my form.
Blended and united, we become gods and spirits.
Emerging as wind and rain, entering to attain longevity.
Follow my commands, heed my orders.
Should you betray me, the wind’s blades shall torment your body.
Should I betray you, your rank shall never rise.
Envoy Zhang [so-and-so], listen carefully, do not forget this covenant.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Transformation Mantra**
My head wears the round of Heaven; my feet tread the square of Earth.
Crowned and girded with the Nine Qi, woven into robes.
The sun as round image, the moon as round light.

To my left, the River Marshal; to my right, the Celestial Stem.
Able to subdue all evil and dissolve misfortune.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Heavenly Peng’s Invocation**
I reverently invoke and submit to the Heavenly Peng General,
Crusher of demon hordes, mighty divine warrior.
With stern crossbows and *kuí*-dragons, descend upon the ritual arena.
Your awe-inspiring radiance shakes Heaven and Earth.
The Twenty-Eight Lunar Mansions, bright stars’ lords;

Three hundred thousand troops all stand guard.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Demon-Quelling Mantra**
The Dark Heaven spreads across the celestial expanse,
Weaving the Han with purple clouds.
Mysterious qi illumines the Three Dawns,
Cinnabar radiance shines upon the Purple Tenuity.
All heavens unfurl their numinous splendor,
The flowing clouds how resplendent.
The divine lamp brightens the Long Star,
The Net of Li spills forth its luminous glow.
Four peaks girded with lofty clouds,
Dark essence shades the Eight Directions.
The Three Primes open the high void,
Orchid gates unfold their layered doors.
Golden walls reflect the Jade Clarity,
Clouds’ beauty marks the celestial precincts.
Winds arise in the Eight Convergences,
Fierce beasts gallop through the clouds.
In the Three Caverns’ bustling courts,
Perfected ones intermingle.
Above, the thousand-mile essence,
In dark purity, towering and majestic.
The Great One of the Celestial Plan gathers and binds,
Wielding the divine brush to seize and command.
The Orthodox Unity treads the flourishing years,
Summoning the myriad spirits to return.
The Duke’s son flanks the silent axle,
The Cavern Yang penetrates the mysterious mechanism.
Feeding on the initial union with the Dao’s *gēng*,
The dragon rises, circling in due course.
The Seven Luminaries unite with the divine kings,
The whirlwind turns upon the wondrous steps.
Bodies agile upon the Dark Ford,
Flying immortals ascend the peaks’ ladders.
Donning cassocks, they enter the divine troops,
Resplendent in crystalline robes.
Dark and bright intermingle in cloudy gatherings,
Flying radiance bears divine communion.
The Pure Peak’s grand assembly,
Wondrously conjoined in the absolute void.
Golden splendor girds the empty chariot,
Winged, the lofty immortals.
Ten thousand reins scatter through the void,
Lush and dark, the upper windows.
The Lords of the Gathered Radiance unite,
The Central King named Nurturing Light.
Luminous clarity begins to birth spirits,
The Nine Perfected unite in pairs.
Wondrous radiance reveals the primal plain,
Following abundance, marking the divine source.
The Muddy Pellet’s Cavernous Origin shines,
Linked pearls in the Crimson Palace.
Primal yang joins the Gate of Life.
Three spirits lead the purple youths,
Seizing and binding the upper realms’ beings.
Flanking the gates, awaiting the bright windows,
Veiled and facing, the dawn’s round.
Splendidly illumined, the Three Spirits’ square,
Abundantly drawing in the living.
Returning the old to youthful ignorance.
The whirlwind’s brilliance shakes the Nine Heavens,
Verdant turns penetrate the cinnabar chambers.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

The mists weave in silent layers beyond,
Their winding glow illumines the resplendent hall.
Wandering the void where transformations arise,
Returning to unite with the Divine Radiance King.
The Dao of immortals delights in life,
The ghostly path delights in misfortune.
Yet who seeks the noble immortal Dao,
Hears not of the ghostly path’s ascendancy.
Chants and songs harmonize with celestial qi,
Guests sing the primal true hymn.
Divine wisdom commands the Crimson Host,
The Five Emperors bear the frost’s chill.
Wielding banners to subdue the myriad demons,
All beings ascend the cloud-capped peaks.
Those who lag behind suffer bitter delay,
While resplendent scriptures inspect the Northern Feng.
Embodiment dissolves into the natural Dao,
Demons vanish—such is your merit.
Sailing the radiant winds with long fans,
Heaven’s tribulations shall never end.
Within the wondrous arises true vision,
Gazing below, the four directions take flight.
The mind unites with true vision,
Lifting high the supreme jade.
Soaring wings await the wondrous union,
Yet profound insight turns sorrowful.
Whistling, gasping, sighing in haste,
Swiftly traversing the nine gates.
Drawing qi to return to the origin,
Merging radiance with the subtle and mysterious.
The Nine Perfected descend in steady brilliance,
Double gates open to a hundred yang.
Thunder and lightning race with hail and lightning,
The five stars rush in shifting motion.
Grasping the tally to command numinous qi,
Surrendering the heart to follow as one.
The battle ends on the demon-sealing path,
Fierce tigers manifest divine might.
Demon masters slay the iniquitous,
Bronze-headed warriors rout the rebellious.
Heaven’s reapers devour ghostly souls,
Bright flames consume the corrupt.
All spirits bow in reverence,
Every sage submits in devotion.
Those who defy our great Dao’s law
Shall be beheaded, their bodies sundered.

The Heavenly Marshal of Black Might,
Emerges in accord with destiny’s grand design.
The Three Barriers of true qi,
Stand lofty as the sun.
Mountains and rivers bow in awe,
The twin luminaries veil their light.
Fierce roars shatter the air,
Golden wings plummet from the sky.
The Five Emperors gird themselves in the divine court,
Myriad spirits receive investiture in the Grand Tenuity.
The Supreme sails the canopy above cinnabar cliffs,
The Eight Radiant Ones spur their chariots at the clouded gates.
Behold the wondrous transformations of the Primordial Cavern,
Return to our Dao in proper ritual.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute!

**Purification of Heaven and Earth Incantation**
Om, chih, hum, ch’a!
Heaven and earth are naturally so.
Impure qi disperses,
Within the cavernous void.
Resplendent and bright, the Great Mystery,
The mighty deities of the eight directions.
**Eastern Mighty Deity, Azure Qi Sovereign,**
General Yang Fang, essence of Wood’s virtue.
Ninety thousand troops,
Azure Dragon General.
Azure banners as their standard,
Encircling the eastern quarter.
Exterminating the qi of green pestilence,
Beheading the spirits of rotten wood.
**Southern Mighty Deity, Vermilion Qi Sovereign,**
General Wang Xiang, spirit of Fire’s virtue.
Thirty thousand troops,
Fire Dragon General.
Crimson banners as their standard,
Encircling the southern quarter.
Sweeping away the qi of red pestilence,
Annihilating the spirits of scorching flame.
**Western Mighty Deity, White Qi Sovereign,**
General Zhou Liang, spirit of Metal’s virtue.
Seventy thousand troops,
White Dragon General.
White banners as their standard,
Encircling the western quarter.
Driving out the qi of white pestilence,
Severing the spirits of dead metal.
**Northern Mighty Deity, Black Qi Sovereign,**
General Zhang Gang, spirit of Water’s virtue.
Fifty thousand troops,
Black Dragon General.
Black banners as their standard,
Encircling the northern quarter.
Cutting off the qi of black affliction,
Burning the spirits of filth’s pool.
**Northeastern Mighty Deity, Azure-Black Qi Sovereign,**
General Yuan Yi, azure-black banners as standard.
Azure-black divine soldiers,
Encircling the northeastern quarter,
Exterminating the spirits of azure-black ghosts.
**Southeastern Mighty Deity, Azure-Red Qi Sovereign,**
General Gao Guang, azure-red banners as standard.
Azure-red divine soldiers,
Patrolling the southeastern quarter,
Exterminating the spirits of red-azure demons.
**Southwestern Mighty Deity, White-Red Qi Sovereign,**
General Xiao Chang, white-red banners as standard.
White-red divine soldiers,
Encircling the southwestern quarter,
Exterminating the spirits of white-red demons.
**Northwestern Mighty Deity, White-Black Qi Sovereign,**
General He Dang, white-black banners as standard.
White-black divine soldiers,
Encircling the northwestern quarter,
Exterminating the spirits of white-black demons.

Above heaven and below,
Banishing malevolent demons.
Let me be naturally so,
Mighty across the eight directions.
Hiss, spit, mumble, sigh!
Swiftly seize, swiftly bind,
Sever and behead the inauspicious.
By the Numinous Treasure’s talismanic command,
Proclaimed to the Nine Heavens.
Qianluo Danna, Cavernous Barrier of the Great Mystery,
Slay demons, bind evil,
Annihilate a myriad ghosts.
Thunder and lightning,
Talismanic command descends.
The Three Realms and Four Palaces,
Mountains and rivers unite.
Stars shift, the Dipper turns,
Moving the Barrier Deities.
Exterminate evil ghosts,
Upon talisman’s arrival, comply.
**Central Mountain Incantation, Supreme Unity of the Mysterious True,**
Uniting the numinous might,
The Mysterious Brightness moves alone.
Summoning winds, shaking clouds,
Enveloping our community,
Let there be thunder,
Sweeping the Three Realms,
Of lawless spirits.
Lu Sha Li Heng, Xu Cha Yan Hui.
The Jade Writ of the Primal Beginning,
Sun and moon traverse together.
The five qi surge and intertwine,
Chariot wheels roll boundlessly.
Swiftly shatter demonic miasma,
Purify the eight extremities.
Heaven brightens, qi clears,
Stars and constellations gleam.
Thunder’s might shakes,
Slaying the malevolent.
Lightning flashes, thunder roars,
Om, chih, hum, ch’a, li—
No delay permitted.
Reciting once,
Demons retreat, years extend.
Marching across the Five Peaks,
The Eight Seas hear as one.
Demon kings bow to the east,
Guarding my chariot.
Malevolence and filth dissolve,
The Dao’s qi ever abides.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command!

**Heavenly Marshal Incantation**
The Great Dao, Mysterious Primal Beginning,
Extends grace from the Supreme Clarity.
The Nine Heavens array their ranks,
The Five Peaks stand in solemn welcome.
Winds and clouds gather for ten thousand miles,
A thousand mountains’ grasses and trees lie flat.
Thunder rumbles past the Northern Sea,
Rainstorms lash the Southern Abyss.
Black Might serves as the central guard,
The Heavenly Marshal appears in the outer camp.
Divine palaces hold jade seals,
The Supreme Unity bears golden crystals.
Fierce generals ride crimson tigers,
Vanguard commanders mount great whales.
Lightning flies with fierce fire,
Thunder drums shake the celestial court.
Orders transmitted to the three generals,
For punitive expeditions, employ the Six Dings.

**Four Directions’ Divine Huoluo,**
Youthful attendants all radiant and bright.
Earth’s net is cast in encompassing weave,
Heaven’s snare moves in encircling flight.
Fire-wheels rise in crimson flame,
Rain-canopies birth sapphire mist.
Shaking, they stir the cosmos’ sway,
Surging, they startle the universe’s sight.
Thirsting, they drain the Eastern Sea dry,
Mightily pressing Mount Tai to its plight.
Tigers respond to white Geng-Xin,
Dragons ride upon azure Jia-Yi’s light.
Sever the heads of raving specters,
Dispel all baleful, venomous sprites.
Lesser ghosts and malevolent wraiths—
How dare they wage war in our sight?
All demonic hordes are swept away,
The human realm rests in eternal night.
Swift as statute and command!

**Heavenly Marshal’s Demon-Slaying Incantation #1**
Dissolved from ghostly legions, one blade’s divine might.
Species annihilated, skies in ruin lie,
Bones shattered, the Four Brightnesses die.
Skeletons blaze beneath the Northern Dipper’s light,
Blood sears in the Emperor Yan’s flame.
Five ghosts’ forms are hewn,
The great celestial axe falls in might.
Should any specter dare approach,
No demon dares resist this sight.
No omen retreats, no curse is cast,
A thousand corpses split in twain.
Ninefold my guard, thirteen legions vast,
Blades gnash with Northern might,
Fury spurs victory o’er heaven’s height.
Southern might subdues the fiendish horde,
Soldiers’ strength in Ding-Tian’s accord.
Four elders’ eyes survey the land,
Teeth green, tongues ashen gray.
Winds drink their flesh, bodies lie slant,
Ghosts devour, demons prey.
Fierce radiance in crimson haze,
Heaven rides the purple qi’s array.
Traces of evil are slain,
The King of Spirits wields his blade’s sway.
Dragons and *kui* drive the solemn chariot,
Three gods in white, their forms display.
The Celestial Bell Emperor grasps my hand,
Beasts vast, their skulls long in fray.
Fiends pale ascend the Supreme,
Eight numina govern, seven powers hold sway.
The Old One of the North, Gao Diao’s might,
Controller of the Capital, Ding’s fifth array.
Youths slay the Primordial Nine,
Heavenly Marshal, Heavenly Marshal, hear my cry!
Swift as statute and command!

**Invocation of the Altar of the Primordial Unity**
I humbly invoke the Generals of the Altar of the Primordial Unity,
Marshal Zhao, Commander of the Golden Wheel.
Thirty-six mighty Divine Kings,
Innumerable soldiers of the Five Thunders and Great Cavern.
Commanding thunder, dispatching lightning to illumine heaven and earth,
Flying talismans shatter temples to seize demonic sprites.
Swiftly seize, swiftly bind malevolent spirits,
Possessing souls, conveying the will’s intent.
Moving mountains, uprooting trees to shake the cosmos,
Wielding whips and ropes to startle gods and ghosts.
Seizing thieves, manifesting forms to disperse legal strife,
Rewarding good, punishing evil to restrain vengeful souls.
Those afflicted by a hundred illnesses—petition and they shall heal,
I possess ten thousand vows that bend to my will’s appeal.
Eight Valiant Kings lead the vanguard,
Four Directions’ mighty forces gather like clouds.
The Celestial Master’s decree—swiftly obey,
Dispatch troops, array formations, unfurl banners high.
Hear my summons and hasten to respond,
Upon achieving merit, ascend to heaven’s hall.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation of the Primordial Beginning**
Danluo, Weiluo, Wuxu, Liutuo.
Supreme Harmony, Supreme Ultimate,
Yin and Yang embrace in accord.
Emerging from being, entering non-being,
Even spirits cannot fathom their course.
Exiting death, entering life,
Transformations arise naturally.
Primordial qi of the undifferentiated,
Mystery within mystery.
Above, it penetrates the celestial taboo,
Below, it pervades the Great Abyss.
Recite once, and chronic ailments heal of their own.
Refining the hun, nurturing the po,
True yang is made whole.
Purify, fast, recite with reverence,
Ten thousand repetitions—ascend as an immortal.
Supreme secret incantation,
Myriad spirits in endless array.
Heart-centered incantation,
Proclaimed again and again.
Greedy Luo’s cavern pact,
Uniting with the Dao in truth.
Jade Clarity’s Supreme Pole,
Brahma-qi in misty profusion.
Dispersing numinous qi, bestowing it upon this servant’s form,
Body and spirit both wondrous, transforming to soar and ascend.
Ascending to the Mysterious Capital,
Commanding the myriad spirits’ sway.
Swift as statute and command!

**Heavenly Marshal’s Decree**
Heavenly Marshal, Heavenly Marshal,
Ancestor of the ten thousand spirits.
Majestic and august is the Great Dao,
Roaming the vastness of the Great Void.
Seated within the Southern Dipper,
Standing amid the Northern Dipper.
Great Marshal of the Purple Tenuity,
Heavenly Thearch’s granted merit.
The Jade Armillary and Jade Balancer,
The Twenty-Eight Constellations.
One qi encompasses all,
Heaven and earth blend as one.
The Five Directions’ Five Dippers,
The demon kings of the Three Realms.
The Heavenly Marshal presides,
His divine qi without peer.
Golden Gates and Jade Chambers,
Possessing mighty divine power.
Enraged, he shakes heaven and earth,
Sun and moon lose their light.
Qi devours the Five Peaks,
Overturning the Four Quarters.
Those who heed my incantation,
Swiftly come and submit.
Those who defy my incantation,
Shall perish in ruin and blight.
Swift as statute and command!

**Summoning the Great Immortal**
Reverently I invoke the Heavenly Marshal,
Master of the Dharma’s gate.
Great Immortal of unfathomable divine might,
Majestic and awe-inspiring without bound.
His fame resounds to the Eight Extremities,
His name shakes the Nine Heavens.
Wielding the Northern Emperor’s decree,
Exercising the Northern Emperor’s authority.
Driving away demons, slaying specters,
Hawks and hounds lead the way.
Regardless of distance,
Slaying without restraint.
Patrolling the world,
Shaking mountains and rivers.
Black clouds surge,
Crimson crests spiral.
Officers and soldiers follow in service,
Hawks and hounds perform their duty.
Should any petty ghost
Dare commit evil and transgress,
Hawks devour, hounds consume,
Swords sever, spears pierce.
I now summon and invite,
Wishing to descend from the Three Heavens.
Marshal of the Dipper’s Star,
Majestic and awe-inspiring without bound.
Three hundred thousand troops,
Greatly amplifying my authority.
Curing illness, dispelling misfortune,
Eradicating evil, banishing calamity.
Once the Great Immortal descends,
The afflicted find peace.
Swift as statute and command!

**Heavenly Peng Ruler Incantation**

Heaven is clear, clear,
Earth is numinous, numinous.
The ten directions of the world,
Vast and boundless.
Within the void,
Above lies the Primal Crystal.
Encompassing the myriad forms,
Governing all spirits.
Its subtle workings shape creation, unfathomable in completion.
Opening heaven, cleaving earth,
Dividing darkness and light.
Once the Great Simplicity scattered,
The myriad kinds flourished.
The Three Powers established their places,
Humanity and justice arose.
Rites and music followed,
Yet wickedness and deceit were born.
The Five Constants confused,
The Four Peoples contended.
Above, no leniency,
Below, no loyalty.
Some became demons, some ghosts,
Some goblins, some spirits.
Rampant and cruel, they poisoned,
Disturbing the lives of the people.
Entire families fell ill,
Kin left solitary.
Below, childbearing ceased,
Above, fathers and brothers perished.
Lives cut short in vain,
Souls and spirits plunged into darkness.
Dao and qi intermingled,
Good and evil obscured.
The Northern Emperor, compassionate,
Took pity on all beings.
Decreed his divine officers,
To sever and decapitate demonic spirits.
Though grievances were many,
The good could be pacified.
The Heavenly Peng Marshal,
Dispersed his traces, divided his forms.
Granted the title "Supreme Emperor,"
Called the Primal Crystal.
Assisting heaven’s transformations,
Manifesting his majestic power.
The Jade Emperor again acted,
Descending from heaven.
Nurturing the multitudes,
Leading them to harmony and peace.
The Great Sage Heavenly Peng,
With three hundred thousand troops.
Returning light, restoring brightness,
Descending to the celestial court.
Patrolling the world,
Hunting and pursuing demonic spirits.
Binding wind and fire,
Ceaselessly capturing.
Slaying all evil,
Boiling every ghost.
Plague officers,
Bound and submissive.
Heaven became clear and refreshing,
Earth became peaceful and tranquil.
People found peace and nourishment,
All things sprouted anew.
Evil was guided to rectitude,
Spirits displayed their power.
The dark city opened for deliverance,
Souls and spirits received new life.
The common folk thrived,
The land was purified.
The Heavenly Peng Marshal,
Decreed the divine ruler,
Bestowing it with fine abilities.
Guarding body and life,
Restraining the myriad spirits.
Within it, the Three Terraces,
Above it, the Seven Stars.
Divine talismans on four sides,
Governing the netherworld.
As the heart directs,
Mountains and peaks crumble.
Thirty-six generals,
Guardian soldiers of the ruler.
Soaring through the skies, inspecting lives,
Moving to stir the Three Clarities.
Delivering people, extending life,
Calming disasters and harm.
Slaying evil, eradicating poison,
Ghosts and specters vanish.
Ascending to immortality, entering sagehood,
Transcending with the ruler.
In harmony with sun and moon,
Dao and qi endure eternally.
Pointing at evil to return to rectitude,
Descending the impure, ascending the pure.
The six heavens’ ghostly thieves,
Upon seeing it, perish and collapse.
The Dao has no high or low,
With the ruler, it prospers.
Climbing mountains, beasts submit,
Entering seas, dragons ascend.
Traveling at dawn, dew scatters,
Traveling at night, the body is light.
Surrounding divine generals,
Bing, Ren, Jia, and Geng.
Summoning clouds and rain,
Thunder crashes and roars.
What spirit does not submit?
What ghost does not tremble?
Those who resist the ruler perish,
Those who honor it live.
Those who defy it are disgraced,
Those who revere it are honored.
Those who venerate it live long,
Those who oppose it perish.
The Marshal’s decree,
The Northern Emperor’s covenant.
Operating the workings of creation,
The Seven Governors align.
Those who violate my decree,
Those who resist my covenant,
Shall be cut into ten thousand pieces,
Forever dead without life.
Swift as statute and command!
