**Northern Emperor’s Divine Ruler Incantation**

The radiant light of the Great Ultimate,
The ruler’s divine workings in motion.
The true qi of the Five Phases,
Revolving endlessly.
The Azure Ruler Spirit King,
Origin of the Primal One.
The Cinnabar Ruler Spirit King,
Moving the luminous to success.
The White Ruler Spirit King,
Assisting the Dao’s majestic power.
The Qi Ruler Spirit King,
Commanding thunder, driving wind.
The Yellow Ruler Spirit King,
All qi harmoniously united.
With a single flourish of the divine ruler,
The Ten Poles are fully connected.
Guarding the Three Origins,
Soaring through the great void.
Decapitating and destroying evil demons,
Dispelling tigers and dragons.

Evil thoughts forever severed,
Swiftly perfecting Daoist merit.
Swift as statute and command!

**Seal Incantation**
The Qian trigram embodies Heaven’s numen,
The Kun trigram bears and moves all.
No deviation from the seasons,
Revolving in endless cycles.
Heavenly soldiers receive my command,
The divine seal of the Six Jia spirits.
They guard my bodily form—
What spirit would not obey?
What demon dare stand in the way?
My seal points to Heaven—Heaven topples;
points to Earth—Earth splits;
points to man—man attains longevity;
points to ghosts—ghosts are annihilated;
points to mountains—mountains crumble;
points to water—water dries;
points to clouds—clouds disperse;
points to trees—trees snap;
points to wind—wind stills;
points to rain—rain ceases.
The August Lord bestows upon me this divine seal,
To transform and subdue you all.
Should any defy my command,
Their four limbs shall be broken and subdued.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation to Summon the Divine Officials**
The Pole Star spirits are upright,
The most revered among gods.
Black mist streams from their nostrils,
Enveloping Heaven and Earth.
In hand they wield golden spears,
Their feet tread upon wheels of fire.
At their sight, evil demons
Shatter in terror and dread.
Hearing this summons,
Hasten forth from the Gate of Heaven,
Come before the altar,
Awaiting orders and tasks.

**Prayer to Dispatch the Divine Officials**
We reverently invoke the Marshal,
Essence of the Pole Star’s might.
You command wind and fire,
Lead the heavenly hosts.
Flinging smoke and hurling flame,
Rolling stones and raising dust.
Sealing mountains and breaching caves,
Traversing the sky in defiance.
Your wrath shakes Heaven and Earth,
The Five Peaks crumble and topple.
Thunder roars and lightning flashes,
Racing like thunderbolts.
The Six Heavens’ Fire Division
Hurls fire and rings bells.
Sky-flying malevolence,
Earth-bound spirits—
All deviant mountain imps,
Seized and captured as one.
Pestilence, plague, and evil ghosts,
Eradicated without trace.
By the August Lord’s decree,
Greatly manifest your numinous power.
Swift as statute and command!

**Talisman Incantation for the Divine Officials**
The Three Heavens issue their mandate,
The Jade Emperor’s edict is clear.
The Four Saints exhort with urgency—
What spirit dare resist?
By the August Lord’s decree,
The Divine Officials are summoned.
To sever evil and misfortune,
Temporarily leaving their posts,
They come to the altar,
Commanding ghosts and spirits,
Severing all inauspiciousness.
Where the heavenly talisman arrives,
Evil calamities are forever severed.
Relieving the people’s suffering,
Greatly bestowing numinous radiance.
Swift as statute and command!

**Iron Barrier Enclosure Incantation**
By the law’s numinous power—
Heaven and Earth move,
Stars and constellations shift,
The Celestial Pass turns,
The Earth’s axis revolves,
Rivers and seas are driven,
Ghosts and spirits are enshrouded.
My art is no trifling matter,
The divine and sacred pierce the Three Clarities.
Ghosts of the Yellow Slaves,
Their bodies crushed to pulp.
Mountain imps and specters,
Reduced to fine dust.
I command eight hundred myriad heavenly soldiers,
Along with the Four Generals,
Sealing the Ghost Gate.
Above, the Heavenly Net Spirit;
Below, the Earthly Snare Generals.
What spirit lies beyond my enclosure?
What ghost escapes my net?
Those who oppose me perish,
Those who submit live.
Swift as statute and command!

**Reverent Summons to Fire Marshal Zhao Yuanri, Ancestral Lord of Primordial Fire**

By solemn decree, I command the Fire Department’s Numinous Marshal, Enclosure-General Zhao Yuanri, to forge iron into a net, cast four great seines to the four quarters, and raise flames to the eight directions—above, piercing the Empyrean; below, linking the Earth’s sovereign; eastward, reaching Fusang; westward, joining the Metal Ancestor; southward, extending to the Sea Gate; northward, touching Fengdu. Now I cast the enclosure in full, dispatching Marshal Zhao. No matter how distant or near, regardless of kinship or estrangement, seize and deliver all inauspicious ghosts to the altar precinct. Comply with the decree and swiftly establish the celestial prison!

**Celestial Prison Incantation**
O numinous celestial prison,
By the August Emperor’s command, proceed!
Lord of the All-Heaven Dharma,
Mighty Celestial Ding.
Five-Thunder Divine Generals,
Great Gods who establish the prison—
Manifest the celestial dungeon,
Imprison the ghosts and spirits.
The celestial prison stands,
The earthly prison is complete.
I summon the heavenly generals
To seize and confine the ghosts and spirits.
Great Gods of the Celestial Gaol,
Divine Lords of the Earthly Gaol—
Seize and confine the wayward ghosts,
Show no leniency.
By the August Emperor’s decree,
Consign them to the ghost encampment.
Swift as statute and command!

**Fire God Incantation**
Dark and mysterious, Heaven and Earth,
Radiant, the sun and moon.
The Five Phases move,
Fierce fire blazes in the four quarters.
Fire reddens Heaven and Earth,
Swiftly, Fire Marshal Gong!
True fire of the upper heavens,
Blazing, soaring through the void.
Five-directional thunder-fires,
Raging flames and dense smoke.
Fire Immortal Generals,
Fire Emperor Jin Zhong—
Molten metal hurled as fire,
Transformations without end.
The Great Sage’s command is issued—
What ghost dares defy?
Plague demons and pestilential ghosts,
Flee without a trace!
*Oṃ viṃ □ṇi ghosta-duṣṭa hūṃ svāhā!*

**Dharma Water Incantation**
Five Numinous Sovereigns,
Essences of the Five Fires—
Return fire to water,
Let rivers and seas grow clear.
Fire bells quake,
Sea dragons cower in alarm.
I draw true *qi*,
Hasten to descend!
Pour into the skin,
Transform the five viscera.
Flow to heal illness,
Sweep away perverse essences.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Treating Fright-Illness**
Dark, dark, dark, dark—
Wind and rain rush in torrents.
Ghosts of fright and malice,
I know your names!
Wind-fright is named *Ding*,
Heat-fright is named *Xin*.
Sudden fright, lingering fright,
Essences of *Shilei*—
Primordial August *qi*,
Swiftly descend upon me!
Sweep away the perverse ghosts,
Hasten to bring peace.
Swift as the primordial descent of statute and command!

**The Third Scroll of the *Highest Three Caverns Divine Incantations* Concludes**

*(Note: The verses of this incantation, except for the final line "Swift as statute and command," are to be read in reverse order.)*

**The Fourth Scroll of the *Highest Three Caverns Divine Incantations*: Thunder Rites and Invocations**

**Incantation for Praying for Clear Skies (Seven Cycles)**
First cycle: Six spirits conceal,
Second cycle: Four malevolent forces vanish.
Third cycle: Yin haze withdraws,
Fourth cycle: Excessive rains cease.
Fifth cycle: Heaven and Earth gleam resplendent,
Sixth cycle: Sun and Moon unite in brightness.
Seventh cycle: Seal the deep pools, lock the seas,
Gather and capture the perverse *qi* of yin haze,
To the judgment of the Five Thunders—annihilation and dissolution of form.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation of the Five Directions’ Barbarian Thunders**
The Dao of Heaven aligns with the True,
Sun and Moon unite in brightness.
Heaven is clear, Earth is tranquil,
The Five Peaks topple and crumble.
Divine spirits assist me,
Heavenly might repels weapons.
Mightily suppress and drive the winds,
Swiftly descend like clouds.
Swift as statute and command!

**Celestial Fire Radiates Light, Earthly Fire Blazes Bright.**
At the divine summons,
Pervade the ten thousand directions.
Radiant illumination shines,
Pursuing and circulating the Five Directions.
My body bears the constellations,
Above, connecting with the Celestial Stem.
Swift as statute and command!

**The Primordial August One commands, the Celestial Stem is seized.**
The Mysterious Beginning’s hidden secrets,
Treasured by the Jade Emperor.
Perfect your wondrousness,
Manifest in the Five Directions.
With a single point of my sword,
Clouds and mist rise high.
Swift as statute and command!

**Heavenly Thunder, Earthly Thunder,**
Voices shake the Eight Directions.
Shattering mountains, toppling peaks,
Resounding to the Great Granary above.
Thunderfire swiftly arrives,
Enveloping clouds, obscuring light.
I now summon you,
All assemble in the Emperor’s realm.
Swift as statute and command!

**Eight Directions’ Abyssal Pools,**
Pervading the ten thousand things.
Communing with Heaven, responding to Earth,
Divine traces appear in the Celestial Stem.
With a single inhalation by the Great Immortal,
All gather at the Celestial Stem.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Purifying the Altar**
Above in Heaven, below on Earth,
Mighty Heavenly Soldiers.
Assist my rites,
Sweep away demonic miasmas.
Foul *qi* swiftly perishes,
Scouring and cleansing demonic vapors.
The altar swiftly purifies,
The Dao’s *qi* eternally abides.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Purifying the Body**
Supreme Perfected and Mysterious Spirits,
The Five Dipper Stars cover my body.
Spirit clear, *qi* refreshed,
Purifying filth, bringing peace.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Purifying the Heart**
The Five *qi* align with the True,
The Qian trigram transforms and changes.
Assisting and guarding,
Heart and spirit without error.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Transforming Form**
By the command of the Three Heavens,
Transform my form.
Azure Dragon, White Tiger,
Attend and guard my body.
Evil ghosts flee far,
True *qi* swiftly arises.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Concealing the Soul and Entering the Dipper**
I receive the Heavenly Master’s covenant of the Heart-Treasure Seal,
Wearing the natural talisman that communicates with the hidden and reaches the netherworld.
Above, penetrating the Grotto-Heavens,
Below, reaching the springs’ gates.
I perform the Yu Step,
Wishing to ascend as an immortal.
The Three Hun Souls’ Lads,
The Seven Po Souls’ Perfected.
Follow my Yu Step,
Wishing to cross the numinous barrier.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Wondrous Application**
First purify the heart, banish stray thoughts.
Sit facing the established direction, toward the breaking point.
Visualize the Three Clarities, gaze into the void.
Summon the Four Saints, the ten thousand soldiers and generals.
Visualize my body, expelling demonic forms.
The Five Dipper’s light conceals my shape.
Step forward on the Celestial Stem, kick back on the scorching path.
My body brightens, the Three Lights descend.
Inhale into the mouth, without error or delusion.
The Fire of the Great Yang descends from Mao,
The Water of the Great Yin descends from You.
The Celestial Stem Star descends from the center.
Purple, white, red—three colors’ forms.
Envelop my body, ten thousand evils chant.
Knock the teeth nine times, the Four Great [Elements] harmonize.
Expel the light of the One Field, my body strengthens.
Inscribe talismans, as the Dharma’s treasury.
Swift as statute and command!

**Heavenly Heart General Incantation**
*Kun ming xing hai wo seng hu, huan hui bing yan wei huang kai...*
The Azure Emperor convenes the spirits,
The White Emperor resides in You.
The Red Emperor nurtures *qi*,
The Black Emperor circulates blood.
The Yellow Emperor presides at the center,
One, five, three transformations.
Dispersing into the ten thousand differences,
Returning wind unites the numinous.
Silent and profound resonance,
Only the True responds.
Dare any evil arise?
Pacify and govern.
By Dharma summon the spirits,
By spirits summon the *qi*.
Congealing naturally,
Circulating through Heaven and Earth.
The Heavenly Heart issues its command,
The ten thousand spirits respectfully heed.
First, the *Luo* slays the malevolent,
Second, the *Tanlang* commands,
Third, the *Jidu* seizes,
*Om* [ ] *li* [ ] *yan* [ ] *svāhā*.
The summoned [general’s name] swiftly arrives.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Commanding the Four Direct Officers**
Heavenly numen, Earthly numen,
Three and Five intersect.
I receive the Emperor’s command,
To investigate and expose perverse essences.
Officers of the Direct Day,
Attending generals and functionaries,
Do not delay or linger,
Hasten to depart, hasten to arrive,
I shall sit awaiting your capture.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Activating the Thunder Bureau**
Heavenly Thunder rumbles in concealment,
Earthly Thunder roars mightily.
Yin Thunder swiftly erupts,
Yang Thunder swiftly resounds.
Thunder’s might startles and shakes,
Dragons and Tigers intertwine.
Sun and Moon arrayed,
Illuminating brightly.
The Twelve Functionaries,
The Five Thunder Envoys.
The Six Jia, Six Ding,
Execute the talismans and proceed.
Swift as statute and command!

**Talisman and Incantation of the Sun’s Essence**
Crimson furnace, cinnabar *qi*,
Mysterious Heaven nurtures essence.
Receiving the firm with the yielding,
Fiery flames, yin’s blossoms.
The Sun’s dawn, primordial radiance,
Named the Great Brightness.
Nine Yangs transform together,
Dual images simultaneously arise.
Congealing the hun and harmonizing the po,
The essence of the Five *qi*.
At the center, the Five Emperors are born,
Riding the light, controlling form.
Gathering and flying with numinosity,
Plucking roots to attain fullness.
At the head’s center, the Dragon harmonizes,
Clad in vermilion, girded in azure.
Reins of birds, flowing mystery,
Rosy clouds reflect the Upper Clarity.
Bestowed the Jade Tablet’s script,
Names engraved in the Golden Watchtower.
Consuming the morning’s blossoms,
Uniting with the Dao in numinosity.
Flying immortals of the Grand Tenuity,
Ascending to the Purple Court.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation of the Sun’s Essence**
The Grand Tenuity’s cinnabar script,
Named the Opening Brightness.
Summon the Sun’s upper hun,
To transform [my] form.
At midday, solemnly adorned,
Emerging from the profound.
Courtyard-flying floral waters,
The Sun’s root, golden essence.
Purple reflections, flowing light,
Named the Five Numinosities.
Swift as statute and command!

**Talisman and Incantation of the Moon’s Essence**
Yellow essence, mysterious radiance,
Primordial yin’s upper *qi*.
Dispersing dense cold winds,
Cultivating the numinous, gathering the stomach.
Vacuous waves, rippling glints,
Upright and cleansed, still vessels.
Moon’s crystal, night’s radiance,
The Mysterious Palace’s supreme treasure.
The Five Palace Ladies,
Each safeguarding their maternal positions.
The Red Heaven flies in,
The Infant Girl follows.
Four yins, three unions,
Light shines in the ten thousand directions.
Harmonizing the hun, restraining the po,
The Five Wombs’ flowing light.
Swift as statute and command!

Riding auroral essence in flight, soaring through the void in the east.
Crowning clouds of numinous radiance,
Fortune graced by the luminous wind.
Left girded with the Tiger Talisman,
Right bearing the Dragon Insignia.
Phoenix-feathered cloud mantle,
Jade pendants and golden earrings.
Lofty trees with branching boughs,
Named the King of Trees.
Divine canopies root-controlling,
Now waning, now shining.
Luminous essence inwardly responds,
Mysterious waters exhale fragrance.
Bestowed the jade tablet’s script,
Inscribed names in the Cloud Chamber.
Ingesting the Moon’s radiance,
In union with the perfected.
Flying immortals of the Purple Tenuity,
Ascending to court the Supreme Emperor.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation of the Moon’s Essence**
Purple Tenuity’s yellow script,
Named the Supreme Mystery.
Dispersing the Moon’s floral waters,
Nurturing the *po*, harmonizing the *hun*.
Within the square, solemn rites,
Issuing from the Mysterious Pass.
Concealing heaven, veiling the moon,
The Five Numinous Ladies.
Ninefold flying lights,
Illuminating the Muddy Pellet.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation for Brush, Ink, Inkstone**
The Sun’s single glance,
Yin ghosts shall be shattered.
Divine cinnabar brightens the eyes,
Nine dews of the Grand Tenuity.
What I now transform,
All myriad evils shall wither.
Seven *qi* form the Dipper,
Three *qi* form the Terrace.
Two stars penetrate with light,
The talisman’s arrival swiftly pursues.
The brush is a divine sword,
The ink a halberd.
The inkstone a dragon pool,
Cinnabar the hundred medicines.
Brush techniques cure illness,
Written sigils—heavenly talismans—wherever they arrive, all obeys.
All demons and evils submit.
Swift as statute and command!

**Incantation of the Three Terraces and Dipper**

**Upper Terrace of Void Essence,**
Preserve my years and span.
**Middle Terrace of Sixfold Purity,**
Guard my bodily form.
**Lower Terrace of Curved Life,**
I bow in audience to the Three Clarities.

**Incantation of the Dipper’s Might**
Head crowned with heaven’s round,
Feet planted on earth’s square.
Hand grasping *Hekui*,
Body armored with *Tiangang*.
Sun as round image,
Moon as round light.
Body clad in the Northern Dipper,
Six pitch-pipes, nine odes.
Able to drive ten thousand spirits,
Dispel all inauspiciousness.
My single command,
Demons and specters perish.
Swift as statute and command!

**Iron Helmet Talisman of Xin the Heavenly Lord**
Facing heaven, iron helmet—celestial fire blazes.
One cast spans ten thousand leagues,
Earth’s fire gleams resplendent.
Head crowned with the Three Terraces,
Below, the Ninefold Excellence is subdued.
Greatly shroud mountain *xiao*—
Souls scatter, spirits vanish.
Lesser shroud specters and sprites—
Sweep away all misfortune.
First shroud: heaven and earth’s murky *qi*,
Second shroud: sun and moon lose their light,
Third shroud: rivers and streams run dry,
Fourth shroud: grasses and trees wither yellow,
Fifth shroud: lightning flashes ten thousand fathoms,
Sixth shroud: wind and rain in all directions,
Seventh shroud: household gates pure and auspicious,
Eighth shroud: divine killers retreat and hide,
Ninth shroud: ancestral dead are gathered,
Tenth shroud: distant plagues and jaundice are eradicated,
Eleventh shroud: tigers and wolves leave no trace,
Twelfth shroud: the ailing regain health.
I invoke the Jade Emperor’s salvation,
Command the thunder deities Deng and Xin,
Zhang and the Five Directions’ heavenly soldiers,
Raise thunderbolts to shroud the unrighteous spirits of the Three Realms.
Shout to the Cloud Heavenly Marshal,
Lead the Five Directions’ thunder generals,
The earth spirits of Mount Feng,
Above spread the heavenly net,
Below lay the earthly snare.
Hasten to shroud and bind—
Let no demon or ghost escape!
Swift as statute and command!

**Summoning Incantation of Xiao Fanshan Zhang the Worthy**
I bear the Emperor’s decree,
Sever and command ten thousand spirits.
Generals Yuan and Yi,
Swiftly manifest your might.
Follow my talisman,
Pursue and seize ten thousand spirits.
*Wangliang* and the Five *You*—
Seize them and bring them to the altar court.
Mountain *chi* and tree guests—
Crushed by stone, burned by fire.
Dare to disobey,
Punishment matches heaven’s law.
Swift as statute and command!

**Summoning Incantation of the Ten Merit Officers of the Primal Unity**
Primal Unity initiates the teaching,
One *qi* divides into the true.
The Six Heavens hold mandate,
Grasping and wielding ten thousand spirits.
Three Terraces cover the body,
Five Dippers conceal the form.
Heavenly axes and halberds,
Guard and protect my true self.
Thunder marshals come and go,
Know my name.
Ten Great Merit Officers,
Hear my command and act!
**Directing Yin and Yang,**
Each has its appointed office.
**Purifying Merit Officer,**
Break filth, dispel miasma.
**Exorcising Merit Officer,**
Bind ghosts, slay spirits.
**Reporting Merit Officer,**
Convey mortal affairs.
**Deliverance Merit Officer,**
Augment destiny, prolong life.
**Guardian Merit Officer,**
Stabilize the *po*, pacify the *hun*.
**Rescue Merit Officer,**
Protect childbirth, hasten delivery.
**Possession Merit Officer,**
Seize the *po*, raise the *hun*.
**Celestial Physician Merit Officer,**
Dispense medicine, fly needles.
**Healing Merit Officer,**
Circulate *qi*, nurture the true.
**Qi-Directing Merit Officer,**
Act as I will, attack and proceed.
Drive out demonic factions,
Assault and refine the afflicted body.
Five viscera, six bowels—
Dare not remain turbid!
Hundred passages flow freely,
Triple Burner harmonized.
One divine talisman,
*Qi* and pulse at peace.
Swift as statute and command!

**Primal Unity Healing Incantation**
Primal Unity’s single *qi*,
Remnant of Gaoxin’s reign.
Entrusted to my disciple,
Swiftly seize, swiftly dispel.
Five Directions’ upright *qi*,
Fill my bodily frame.
All Great Merit Officers,
Act as I will, attack and proceed.
Solemnly summon the Ten Great
Merit Officers to needle and lance.
Lesser officers spread *qi*,
Divine healers attend illness.
Celestial Physician Great Sage,
At my call, instantly arrive,
At my summons, instantly attend.
Ten thousand incantations, ten thousand spirits—
Dare not disobey my command!
Dare to disobey,
Punishment lies in thunder’s wrath.
Swift as statute and command!

Before Heaven, before Earth,
Primal Ancestral *Qi*.
Sever death, ascend to life,
Eternal life in the world.
Jade Emperor’s Heart Seal—
Ghosts and spirits all retreat.
Upholding the Three Realms,
Commanding the ten thousand spirits.
Primal Origin’s Master Seal,
Myriad gods obey its decree.

**White Serpent General’s Exorcism of Evil**
White Serpent’s might and flame,
Transforming without bound.
Gaze upward to the heavens,
Sun and moon lose their light.
Gaze downward to the earth,
A hundred grasses wither yellow.
Evil demons that behold it,
Crushed to death, flee in mourning.
In my grasp I wield its power,
Slaying monsters, dispelling misfortune.
No matter far or near,
Seize them and bring to the altar.
By my command,
Swiftly obey without delay.
Swift as statute and command!

**Summoning Wind Wheel Zhou General**
Chaos vast and surging,
*Qi* first divided.
In the North there is a general,
Named Wind Wheel.
A thousand *zhang* tall,
Iron-faced general.
Raising clouds, spewing mist,
Born in an instant.
With a host of ten thousand,
Scouring malevolent spirits.
Whether demons or ghosts,
Whether goblins or spirits,
Whether far or near,
Whether kin or neighbor—
Wind Wheel’s single sweep,
No ghost escapes its form.
By imperial decree I command,
Dare you not comply?
Hasten to stir and move,
Show yourself clearly.
Swiftly come, swiftly come, swiftly come!

**Yu Step to Ward Off Tigers and Wolves**
Four verticals, five horizontals,
Six Jia, Six Ding.
Chiyou governs the path,
Meng Tian’s marching soldiers.
Traversing all under heaven,
Twisting halberds in reverse.
All tigers and wolves,
Bandits and thieves,
All vicious and evil—
Gather beneath my *kuigang*,
Motionless, inactive.
Swift as statute and command!

**Offering to the Six Ding**
Six Ding, celestial warriors,
Hear my prayer and attend.
By the power of the Jade Emperor’s decree,
Descend to my altar this day.
Swift as statute and command!

What Heaven nurtures,
What Earth brings forth.
Above, receive the divine talisman—
Thus may you attain long life.
Immortal sages assist the self,
Jade maidens sustain the form.
The twenty-eight constellations,
Record the names of the starry ranks.
Five directions, five colors:
Black, white, red, azure.
The Yellow Emperor of the Center,
Stands beside me as one.
After receiving the talisman,
May all wishes be fulfilled.
Crush and scatter the myriad spirits,
For they know themselves untrue.
Do not oppose my truth,
For they know themselves not divine.
Do not defy my divinity—
Advance, and be enfeoffed;
Retreat, and be beheaded.
Swift as statute and command!

**Six Ding Protection Mantra**
Ren Gao guards me,
Ding Chou preserves me.
Ren He delivers me,
Ding You keeps me whole.
Ren Can governs the soul,
Ding Si nurtures the spirit.
The canopy of Great Yin,
Earth’s gate and Heaven’s door.
I tread the Yu Step,
True Person of the Dark Maiden.
In the Hall of Light, I sit and lie,
Concealed, hidden, my form obscured.
Swift as statute and command!

**Summoning Marshal Zhu**
Om hum hum!
By the Jade Emperor’s decree, Zhu Yan swiftly descends,
The ringing bells urgently summon him on wind and cloud.
His eyes like rings radiate sun and moon,
His black face, fierce and mighty, shatters Kunlun.
Hearing the command, he turns from the imperial palace,
By edict, he flies in haste to the altar court.
Aid my great Dao in reviving the true teaching,
I charge you to interrogate and strike the faithless.
Should any wicked sorcerer act against the Dao,
A single blow of the golden hammer seizes their soul.
Seize and bind the living soul to the deputy’s body,
Let them delude themselves, attach themselves, and be interrogated in life.
The six caves’ vengeful demons are shattered to dust,
The ten directions’ plagues and pestilences turn to ash.
Om hum hum!
By the Jade Emperor’s decree, Zhu Yan swiftly descends,
I now summon you, my stalwart general,
I now summon you, my stalwart spirit.
Om hum hum! By edict, swiftly descend!
A thousand leagues’ response is here and now—
Swiftly descend, swiftly descend, hasten to descend!
Swift as statute and command!

**Dispatching Marshal Zhu**
Mysterious Thunder’s Dark Lord,
Exalted by Heaven’s command.
The Jade Emperor’s crimson banner,
Commands the thunder hosts.
Whirlwinds and sudden rains,
Seething clouds surge and boil.
His form swells, drums and dances,
Traversing the sky in defiance.
Mountains crumble, stones split,
His might subdues Heaven and Earth.
Should any living person resist,
Swiftly possess their body.
Golden hammers wildly swing,
Iron rods cross and clash.
Flying Heaven’s demon kings,
Seized alive and devoured whole.
Thunderbolts streak through the void,
Decapitating the wicked hordes.
The sorcerer’s seven generations,
Their gall shatters, their hearts topple.
Flying lariats bind the six directions,
Severing and binding the yang souls.
Hurl fire a thousand miles,
Break filth, dispel miasma.
A thousand evils dare not approach,
Ten thousand wickednesses hide their forms.
By the Supreme Emperor’s edict,
Act with utmost haste!
Swift as statute and command!

**Talisman Water Mantra**
The Five Thunders of the Northern Dipper,
Darkness resounds with Heaven’s drums.
Wind Earl sweeps away pestilence,
Lightning Mother dispels suffering.
Thunderclaps strike down demonic spirits,
Rain Master sends forth dharma rain.
It washes into the Triple Burner,
Clearing and cooling the organs and viscera.
Where heavy, instantly lighten;
Where damaged, instantly mend.
Where hot, instantly cool;
Where congested, instantly disperse.
Where endangered, instantly secure;
Where pained, instantly cease.
Swift as statute and command!

**Thunder Sword Mantra**
The *gang* spirit and the *xun* wind,
Thunder and lightning, vast and obscure.
The Five Dragons’ thunderous quake,
The tortoise’s majesty from the Northern Sea.
Power boundless and weighty,
All generals bear and welcome.
Summon the thunder’s roar,
Let wind follow thunder’s charge.
Hasten!

**Thunder Command Mantra**

**Commander of All Thunder**
The Commander of All Thunder executes decrees by mandate.
Marshal Bo Wen, fierce officer and Han subject,
Crushes mountains and overturns peaks,
Exhales mist and summons clouds.
The Three Bureau’s mighty generals,
The Eight Gates’ venomous thunder.
Strike the celestial drum at once,
To hunt and seize demonic spirits.
Subdue demons and suppress evil,
Bringing great peace to the earth.
Swift as statute and command!

**Thunder Talisman Mantra**
The Great One in obscurity,
Obeys the decree and moves swiftly.
Thunder’s generals and officers,
Thunder’s celestial soldiers, arise!
Let thunder erupt without delay,
By imperial command fulfilled.
Who dares defy this order,
Offends the celestial perfected.
To violate the Emperor’s decree,
Is to rebel against the Highest Clarity.
Swift as statute and command!

**Heaven-Splitting Mantra**
Red horns bear the script,
Northern Emperor of Kunlun.
Soaring through heaven, overturning earth,
Slaying and vanquishing demonic spirits.
The Supreme Emperor decrees,
Summoning all spirits at once.
Swift as statute and command!

**Invoking Thunder to Bring Rain Mantra**
Essence of the Northern *Ren* and *Gui*,
Great Fire Bell of the South.
Roaring with thunder and lightning,
Breathing forth wind and clouds.
Seizing wind, hurling water and fire,
In the palm, thunderbolts arise.
Shaking the pillars of Kunlun,
Rivers and seas surge in turmoil.
Guan Bo smashes mountains and peaks,
A hundred streams pour like torrents.
Mists of water and fire congeal,
A deluge fills the land.
None may defy my command,
Report to the Four Spirits on high.
Whoever violates my decree,
Rebels against the Highest Clarity.
The Heavenly Emperor shall destroy your body,
Fengdu shall execute your form.
Swift as statute and command!

**Subduing Earth Spirit Mantra**
Stellar smoke responds in kind,
Spirits of the Five Lands and Earth Altar.
Unleash numinous power, scatter evil,
Black records take thunderous form.
Hearing this, their courage shatters,
Answering the summons, they hide their forms.
Those who oppose me shall die,
Those who resist shall be punished.
At the first sign of divine might,
Move swiftly as a decree!
Let thunder erupt without delay,
Let celestial stars arise at once.
Swift as statute and command!

**Breaking the Xun Mantra**
Thunderbolts shake and quake,
Lightning and fire burst forth in radiance.
Crossing *Qian*, treading the Dipper,
Striding the *Kui*, stepping the *Gang*.
The Five Thunders erupt in haste,
Inner lightning flashes in brilliance.
Illuminating the four seas to a boil,
Shining through Fusang to its core.
Thunder gods and all generals,
Arise swiftly from the *Xun* direction.
Swift as statute and command!

**Opening the Qian Mantra**
Commander of Heaven’s Thunder,
Resplendent through heaven and earth.
Divine dragons lend their guard,
Mountains and peaks crumble and fall.
Demonic spirits and spectral fiends,
Dare not bare their scales.
Thunder Lord strikes with force,
Shattering their forms to nothing.
Ghosts and monsters swept away,
The human realm rests in peace.
Swift as statute and command!

**Concealment Mantra**

**Swift Concealment Mantra**
Nana Yiyi,
Left girded by the Southern Dipper,
Right girded by the Northern Culmen,
Dwelling in the river as my abode.
Heaven overturns, earth inverts,
Nine paths plunged into darkness.
East becomes West,
South becomes North.
Let the demonic spirits,
Their minds bewildered in confusion.
Those who pursue me,
Find no path to tread.
Chasing me by chariot,
Break their axles asunder.
Pursuing me on horseback,
Blind their two eyes.
Seeking me in flight,
Rend their two wings.
Chasing me on foot,
Swollen be their two feet.
Heaven overturns, earth inverts,
Jade pathways all obstructed.
Coming, no trace;
Going, no track.
The true mechanism of heaven and earth,
Beyond the ken of ghosts and spirits.
Bright stars and Northern Dipper,
Repel foes a myriad leagues away.
Yellow Spirit, Yue Chapter,
Slay demons and dispel misfortune.
Those who hate me perish,
Those who betray me die.
Oxherd and Weaver,
Sever the two rivers apart.
Swift as statute and command!

**Opening the Earth’s Veins Mantra**
Summoning the Five Thunder Lords,
Wind and fire swiftly interflow.
Splitting open the *Xun* gate asunder,
Yin *qi* ascends to the empty sky.
Grand Unity’s flying radiance,
Light mirrors the fire-thunder’s surge.
True *qi* descends from the nine heavens,
Thunder erupts, shaking the *Xun* palace.
I now enact this talisman and incantation,
Grasping the *Gang*, riding the nine dragons.
Green Waves Heaven issues its decree,
Rain falls in an instant.
Thunder Lords, arise with haste,
Thunder’s command brooks no delay.
Demons and fiends shattered into mud,
Thunderbolts strike the root of evil.
Should you but slight the Grand Unity’s command,
I shall seize you and dispatch you to Northern Feng.
Swift as statute and command!

**Divine Gnat Mantra**

**Swift Fire Praying for Snow Mantra**

Hasten! Hasten! As the law commands.

**Treating Malevolent Influences Spell**
I with Heaven’s Lord eliminate ten thousand calamities,
Transform my body in the human realm to become Ghost King.
Body ten *zhang* tall, square teeth,
Bronze fangs, iron claws, flying lightning.
Before drives thunderclap, behind cauldrons of boiling water,
Swift thunder, wielding lightning, tread the Celestial Stem.
Grass and trees wither and shrivel, utterly destroyed,
Collapse cliffs, split rocks, sever bridges.
Eyes flash and illuminate heaven and earth,
One rage boils the seas, topples the Five Peaks.
Slay demons, devour iniquities, extirpate fierce and strong,
Seize and capture, sever inch by inch, cut off disasters.
Summon clouds, bring rain in an instant,
Five Directions’ thunder and lightning arise with dragon patterns.
I wield the divine spell—none dare stand before,
*Wangliang* and demonic essences all perish.
Hasten! Hasten! As the law commands.

**The Fourth Scroll of the Most High Three Caverns Divine Spells Concludes**

**The Fifth Scroll of the Most High Three Caverns Divine Spells**
**Prayers, Exorcisms, and Treatments: Various Spells**

**Summoning the Dark Altar**
Pray to the Dark Altar Marshal,
Wielding the rope, brandishing the whip.
Commanding the Eight Generals,
Bravely charging ahead.
Holding halberds, wielding swords,
Golden drums shake heaven.
Hearing my summons,
Instantly descend before the altar.
Golden Wheel Commander-in-Chief,
Dragon-Tiger General Zhao,
Divine Empyrean Swift-Seizing General,
Subduing and Driving Might Spirit.
Above receives the Reverent Emperor’s command,
Below examines mortal affairs.
Iron chains clatter in the heavens,
Iron whips crack upon the earth.
Riding dragons, roaming sea isles,
Mounting tigers, traversing the cosmos.
Left has the Heavenly River General,
Right has the Four Seasons Spirits.
Before has the Yuanbo Envoy,
Behind has the Wenye Lord.
Eight Extremes’ Eight Kingly Generals,
Four Directions’ Four Assembled Soldiers.
Majestically wielding dharma power,
Illustriously manifesting divine numen.
*Nine hūṃ □ hóu lī, decree and bind ghosts and spirits.*
Firmly bind, say firmly bind,
*Hóu □ om du □.*
Flying talismans to evil spirits’ temples,
Seize and capture demonic essences.
Red fire burns away pestilential evils,
Flying smoke pursues ghostly plagues.

Those who conceal their names among evil thieves,
Those who punish the unjust—
Examine the unvirtuous,
Hold fast to the rebellious to save living beings.
At the command’s descent, winds and clouds converge;
As the dharma moves, stars and constellations dim.
Leading troops down to the mortal realm,
To deliver all sentient beings.
Myriad spirits uniformly receive the decree,
Village altars array ranks in welcome.
I now summon you—
Swiftly manifest your true form.
*Hasten, hasten, as the law commands!*

**Summoning the Fierce Soldier Spell**
Fierce soldiers, mighty officers,
Radiant and majestic in numinous power.
Wielding halberds and brandishing swords,
They grant life or kill without mercy.
Furious and ferocious,
Rampant and savage.
Severing heads, blood dripping,
Devouring ghosts and consuming essences.
Eyes bulging, glaring fiercely,
Breaking camps and burning encampments.
Roaming freely, manifesting everywhere,
Dominating the land with towering might.
By the Orthodox Unity’s decree,
Retribution is clear and distinct.
Hearing my call,
Hasten here at once.
*Hasten, hasten, as the law commands!*

**Summoning the Two Harmonious Saints Spell**
I invoke the Two Harmonious Saints,
Whose words are gentle and conciliatory, saving sentient beings.
Jade pendants tinkling, radiant with rosy clouds,
From dark clouds emerge their twin forms.
Their beauty rivals Xi Shi, brows like drooping willows,
Bodies draped in crimson robes, auspicious qi billowing.
Fragrant winds carry rare perfumes,
Rich and lush, scenting the earth.
Feet treading golden lotuses, each step blooming,
Hands grasping the Emperor’s seal, dispelling obstacles.
Ever compassionate, bringing joy and fear,
Swiftly harmonizing the five directions for prosperous trade.
With trunks like elephants’ and noses like tusks, they lead the way—
Whoever chants the Harmonious Saints’ spell,
*Oṃ hūṃ □ hóu lī hūṃ □ hóu lī.*
Let the Two Saints swiftly harmonize and gather.
*Hasten, hasten, as the law commands!*

Encounter evil, seize and capture.

Issues its decree without pause.
Swift as wind and fire,
Rapid as thunder’s charge.
Ghosts perish, humans thrive,
Heaven and earth grow solemn and pure.
*Hasten, hasten, as the law commands!*

August Heaven births all things.
Ascending to the Three Heavens,
Dragon spirits divide their paths.
Thunder spirits rise to Heaven,
Wind Earls blow and spread clouds.
Rain Masters sprinkle sweet dew,
Thunderclaps shake the celestial court.
Five Dragons descend with rain,
Nine Rivers hasten with rain.
Five Lakes move in great mist,
Eight Winds overturn the seas.
Stream and spring dragons bear,
Escorting the thunder decree,
Striking drums in the celestial court.
Pan Emperor Pan Luo,
Jiepo Luo Ji Emperor,
Luo □ Po Luo Jie Emperor,
Po Luo Long Jie Emperor.
All dragons bring rain,
Rescuing and aiding all people.
Ascend through effort to high rank,
Five Thunders descend with rain.
Five Thunder Messengers,
Thunderclaps shake Heaven and Earth.
Crushing mountains, toppling peaks,
All things flourish together.
Upper Clarity brings salvation,
No delay is permitted.
Hasten as the statute commands!

**Heavenly Chapter Eighty-Six-Sentence Ghost-Terrifying Incantation**
August Heaven births me,
August Earth bears me.
Thunder and lightning assist me,
Immortal Palaces establish my being.
I summon sun and moon,
Grasp and wield the stars.
Heavenly hail and wind hail,
Thunder’s voice is distinct.
Dark and tumultuous,
Thunderclaps shake Heaven.
Left hand presses Heavenly Chapter,
Right hand presses Jade Numinosity.
Seventy-two generals,
Bear and escort me on my way.
Heaven’s gates open for me,
Earth’s doors clear my path.
Seventy-two generals,
Bear and enforce the command.
Three thousand six hundred spirits,
Ever at my side.
Golden Flower Fire Wheel,
Original Life Water Numinosity.
Scattered in Jasper Pool,
At a single thunderclap.
Heavenly wandering, earthly wandering,
Azure wandering, Five Wanderings.
Transmit my command,
Bear the rank, seize the dragon.
Rivers and streams lengthen me,
Wind Earls shake and stir,
Rain Masters churn the court.
Heavenly thunder rises,
All things flourish together.
August Heaven sends rain,
Dragon and sea’s gate.
Flowing sands, great waters,
Seven Slayers move as one.
August Heaven births the human Dao,
August Heaven severs the ghostly Dao.
Pan Emperor Jie Pan Luo,
Jie Po Luo Jie Luo,
Jie Luo Po Long,
Rescuing and aiding all people.
Crushing mountains, overturning seas,
Command issues from Green City.
Chanting, gasping, whispering,
Great Dew, Eight Winds,
Mourning the sea, moving through streams.
Five Directions’ thunderclaps,
Crushing dragons take flight.
East Sea Crone-Dragon,
South Sea Fire-Emerging,
West Sea White Sand,
North Sea Wave-Flipping,
Central Sea Great Water,
Five Lakes crushing peaks.
Poyang, Banana Lake,
Twelve Stream Perfected.
Poison dragons, howling dragons,
Laoyue Ba Poison.
By numinous power summoned,
Follow the voice, follow the incantation.
Mountains and rivers emit qi,
Hundred spirits take form.
Northern Capital’s Water Prefecture,
Yan Lord guards the ice.
Lunar Yin, Lunar Brilliance,
Metal Mother sets forth.
Three Officials open the locks,
Five Emperors unite in trust.
Dragons fly, lightning runs,
Metal Tigers, Fire Decrees.
Vast Masters, Great Flower,
Flowing Essence, Grotto Numinosity.
What spirit does not obey?
What command goes unfulfilled?
Above is the Great One,
Ten Earths’ numinous officials.
Purple Void Mystic Sage,
Bear the command and proceed.
Golden Register’s secret name,
Descends from the thunderous court.
Defy the thunder and be shattered,
Obey the thunder and flourish.
Body emits golden radiance,
Ascend into the imperial court.
Hasten as the statute commands!

**Great One’s Three Heavens Capital Incantation**
I bow to the Central Heaven’s host of luminous stars,
Splitting open primordial chaos with thunderous roars.
Assisting Heaven to erect the pillars of Heaven and Earth,
Rending Earth, overturning Heaven, shaking the Xun Gate.
Azure Emperor’s Blue Youth transmits the command,
Heaven’s decree issues in thunderous roars.
Now I employ all star marshals,
Big Dipper turns, stars shift and clash in flight.

**Nine Heavens’ Dharma-Holding Sage Mother Incantation**
Tortoise Terrace Sage Mother, greatly compassionate,
Issuing Dharma to connect with Heaven, universally saving people.
Lunar Yin and Lunar Brilliance transmit the teachings,
Eleven Great Luminaries govern thunder and lightning.
Winnowing Basket and Net stars’ winds and rains wing thunder’s rise,
Creating and transforming the myriad things to full completion.
Now I return six times to the Mysterious Heaven’s Record,
Flying and running with divine talismans, summoning the Clashing Stars.
Metal, Wood, Earth stars with Water and Fire,
Divine mechanisms wondrously employed, shaking the celestial court.
Intersecting beginnings and ends with comets and broom stars,
Great One’s honor holds great power.
Now I send flying talismans ahead on the path,
Heed the command, follow the summons, hasten swiftly.

**Northern Dipper Establishment Incantation**
Northern Direction’s Thunderclap Messenger,
Thunder Duke Great Spirit,
Establishing the Dipper, wielding the banner,
Eradicating evil, eliminating forms.
Thunder roars with decree—
Swiftly descend to the imperial court!
Five Peaks and Four Waterways,
Follow my Dipper’s procession.

Alone I roam through Heaven and Earth,
All myriad spirits attend and follow.

**Dusk and Heaven Dipper-Wall Incantation**
Dusk veils Heaven and Earth, thunder quakes, lightning flashes,
The Dipper’s pivot turns, sundering Qian and Kun.
Three thousand six hundred Thunder Generals,
Follow the Three Terraces, arrayed with the luminaries.
The Sun-Crushing Spirit descends straight to the deep sea,
Summoning the Great Yin to overturn the seas and return to the source.
Transforming divine powers, erasing ghosts and spirits without trace,
Dispatching the Five Terraces to shatter souls and sunder forms.

**Fivefold Blackness Incantation**
Heaven dims dim,
Earth dims dim,
People dim dim,
Ghosts dim dim.
Heaven blackens black,
Earth blackens black,
People blacken black,
Ghosts blacken black.
Heaven’s head is severed,
Earth’s head is severed,
People’s heads are severed,
Ghosts’ heads are severed.
Heaven sinks deep,
Earth sinks deep,
People sink deep,
Ghosts sink deep.
Great lakes sink deep,
Lesser lakes sink deep,
Heaven sinks, Earth sinks.
Ten thousand leagues of raging winds blow shut the eyes of demons,
Ten thousand leagues of black winds block and sever the paths of ghosts.
People leave no shadow to seek,
Ghosts leave no trace to follow.
Ten roads all closed,
Nine roads all cut off.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Jade Emperor’s Heart Incantation**
Metal, Wood, Earth, Water, Fire—pestilence,
Nine Springs’ plague spirits Qin Bowen, Yang Bowen,
Heat spirit Liu Bowen, Cold spirits Mao Wenwu.
The Most High issues decree:
Messengers of the Five Directions,
Above the Six Heavens,
Enforce the law and depart swiftly.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

Five Pestilences and plagues,
Consigned to the Seven Stars.
Eastern Dipper records ghosts,
One dispatch to the Celestial Court.
Western Dipper gathers souls,
Knowing your names.
Hasten to disperse, hasten to scatter,
Celestial Emperor’s officers and soldiers.
Spread nets and weave snares,
Mounting fire wheels.
Devouring demons, consuming ghosts,
Binding your malevolent spirits.
What spirit does not submit?
What ghost dares resist?
Incant the spirit, spirits self-diminish,
Incant the ghost, ghosts self-perish.
Thousands upon thousands, sever heads,
Myriads upon myriads, shear forms.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Dispelling Pestilence Incantation**
Hark! With solemn decree:
Eastern Green Pestilence ghosts,
Spirits of rotting wood.
Southern Red Pestilence ghosts,
Spirits of blazing fire.
Western White Pestilence ghosts,
Spirits of dead metal.
Northern Black Pestilence ghosts,
Spirits of filthy pools.
Central Yellow Pestilence ghosts,
Spirits of dung and earth.
Four seasons, eight solar terms,
Thriving and transforming into life.
Spirits not inwardly nurtured,
Outwardly become perverse essences.
Now I know your names,
Recognize your forms and shadows.
Pestilence ghosts of the Five Directions,
Yellow Slaves, Seven Sons, Hundred Mulberry Brothers,
All sundry miscreants—
Banish your traces, erase your forms.
By this talismanic command,
Act with utmost urgency.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Sweeping Incantation**
Five-Thunder Divine Kings dispel misfortune,
A single thunderclap—perverse spirits vanish.
Fiery chariots ten thousand fathoms high burn and slay the Yellow Pestilence,
Fierce winds sweep and scatter them to the eight directions.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Severing Pestilence Incantation**
I am the Sun’s radiance, my might shakes the Nine Heavens.
Golden fire blazes ahead, flying dragons coil around Qian.
The Yellow Spirit wields the executioner’s axe, the jade celestial chart in hand.
Five Stars and Five Dipper Lords harmonize the Seven Primes.
Gather and seize the Nine Uglies, behead and slaughter the Five Pestilences.
Sweep away evil and malice, banish misfortune.
You must depart at once, submit to my Northern Dipper’s might.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Heavenly and Earthly Pestilence, Harmonizing Pestilence Explained**
When earthly spirits spread pestilence, Heaven’s pardon precedes them.
When demonic forces spread pestilence, their traces and smoke are obliterated.
The Most High issues this decree to preserve human longevity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Expulsion Incantation**
The Most High of the Mystic Capital, four covenants with flying talismans.
Nine Perfected lead the vanguard, Heavenly Soldiers drive from behind.
Five Thunders and Eight Generals, Six Jia True Talismans.
Soaring through heaven and hurling to earth, they capture and seize malevolent spirits.
Seize the perverse, punish the wicked—rebels are swiftly executed.
Heavenly Pestilence Year-Officers, receive the Emperor’s writ.
Look up and obey the talismanic command—you may not linger.
Quickly gather the disease toxins, release the afflicted bodies.
Dispel calamity, dissolve disaster, strike their names from the ledger of death.
Should any dare defy this command, swiftly dispatch them to Fengdu.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Beheading Pestilence Incantation**
Divine Empyrean Jade Clarity, Heavenly Soldiers of the Ten Directions.
Clad in azure jade armor, dragon-washed tiger-sashed.
They capture and restrain the myriad demons, hunt down and seize the spirits.
As the incantation decrees, the Dao reverses and they stealthily draw near.
Retribution, retribution—lifespans remain unshaken.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Cloud Net Incantation**
The Cloud Net descends from Heaven’s Record,
Divine radiance gleams in the Purple Tenuity.
Seven Perfected return to the Emperor’s throne,
Nine Dipper Lords inhabit the Jade Void.
The Purple Canopy crowns the Empyrean Ridge,
Mysterious essence illumines the eight corners.
Above dwell the Nine Morning Guests,
Chanting and reciting hidden feather-script.
They soar and roam the northern wastes,
Dwelling long between heaven and earth.
Reining in at the Dark Feather Terrace,
They traverse the Nine Heavens’ domains.
The cavernous depths stretch far and profound,
The Cloud Net ascends through empty space.
Below, the Perfected Adepts gather,
Gazing upward to summon the Jade Morning Companions.
Three cycles ascend to the Yang Brightness,
Nine revolutions enter the cavernous wilds.
With lofty steps they mount the Emperor’s court,
Singing long the Dragon-Flight Song.
The Jade Morning reflects the northern wastes,
Jasper branches and kingfisher hues hide in the hills.
The Ninefold Numinous Terrace arises in emptiness,
Resplendent and shining to the farthest reaches.
The Heavenly Pass revolves with doubled brightness,
The kalpa’s assembly is repeatedly enmeshed.
Mounting my feathered chariot,
I stride across the Weaving Maid’s River.
Preserving the numinous in empty transformation,
Forever forgetting the world’s abundance.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Eradicating Toxins Incantation**
Central Earth Mansion, Great Star Lord,
Wielding your sword, you guard Heaven’s Gate.
Below, the multitudes suffer calamity and disaster—
Pray, let the talisman arrive and terrify the ghosts and spirits.
Should any stubbornly resist and defy,
The net of heaven’s fire shall burn their souls.
Those who offend the Earth Sovereign’s baleful stars,
Shall find fortune and misfortune fleeting.
Should any pestilence persist in defiance,
I shall open the Heavenly Eye and unleash Heaven’s wrath.
Dragon-Headed Envoys bear the talisman forth,
Retribution manifests, the Emperor’s glory revealed.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Talismanic Edict of Empowerment**
Supreme is the Great Dao,
The Primordial Mandate of the Origin.
Divine winds stilled, silence reigns,
Mountains and peaks veil themselves in clouds.
The Primal One’s subtlety and wonder,
Its essence harmonizes with nature.
A single qi flows and circulates,
Nurturing and fostering all beings.
Those who follow me shall prosper,
Those who oppose me shall perish.
By the Supreme’s edict,
Thus it is proclaimed and obeyed.

**Summoning Thunder Incantation**
Empowered by *hūm*, *chà*, *dū*! □ Thunder Incantation,
By decree, summon the Thunder Gods—*hūm*—piercing heaven and earth!
*Chà*! □ Thunder’s radiance,
By imperial command, seize and manifest your true form!
*Oṃ*! *Chēn*! □ Seize!
*Lai tā*, *suōpó*! Seize!
Wood-Wolf Spirit □, Fire-Bell Spirit □,
Thunderbolt Spirit □, Sudden-Fire Spirit □,
Fierce Officer Spirit □, Swift Spirit □,
Jade-Flower Spirit □, Cloud-Raising Spirit □,
Wind-Calling Spirit □!
*Oṃ oṃ*, by edict, swiftly appear!
By imperial decree, swiftly appear!
*Oṃ sān mǎn dōng nǎ*! Seize!
*Yǎ*! □ Wind-Calling Spirit,
Hasten from the Xun Palace!
By the edict of the Three Heavens,
Your servant, so-and-so, by command summons you—descend swiftly, descend swiftly!
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

The Divine Empyrean and Jade Clarity,
Kneading jade, refining gold.

Ghosts wail, spirits tremble.

That all things may attain longevity.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

True qi arises of itself,
Crimson-scripted jade characters,
The Eight Mighty Dragon Scripts.
Preserving and governing the kalpas,
Ensuring Heaven’s eternal endurance.
Curing illness, severing evil,
All beings dwell in peace.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Big Dipper Incantation**
The Nine Stars of the Northern Dipper,
Great deities of the Central Heaven.
Above, they attend the Golden Palace,
Below, they tread upon Kunlun.
Regulating the cosmic order,
Governing Heaven and Earth.
Great Pivot, Greedy Wolf,
Giant Gate, Wealth Repository,
Literary Brilliance, Integrity and Chastity,
Martial Brilliance, Breaker of Armies.
Exalted Jade Emperor,
Purple Tenuity Emperor Lord.
Encompassing the great celestial sphere,
Penetrating even the tiniest dust.
What calamity shall not be eradicated?
What fortune shall not be attained?
The Primordial Emperor’s true qi,
Come and merge with my body.
Wherever the Celestial Pivot points,
Day and night it turns without cease.
The common folk, petty and unenlightened,
Seek the Dao and yearn for the numinous.
May they behold your august presence,
And forever safeguard their longevity.
The Three Terraces’ ethereal essence,
The Six Pure Ones’ curved life.
They give me life, they nourish me,
They protect my body and form.
□□□□□□□ Exalted Emperor.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

The Emperor’s talismanic mandate,
The Northern Dipper’s pivotal mechanism.

Radiant upon the clouded thoroughfares.
The true qi descends in concealment,
All evil is eradicated and destroyed.
Protecting the body, bestowing wealth and nobility,
Fortune and prosperity follow in its wake.
Dissolving calamities, delivering from distress,
Any anomaly shall be instantly removed.
The Pivot Star’s true qi,
Sweeps away all without remainder.
The descending talismanic mandate,
Ascends to the Jade Clarity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

The Supreme’s Mystic Capital,
The Black Statute’s true talisman.

Malevolent forces and specters are destroyed.

**Edict of the Five Earths Incantation**
Three beams, nine pillars,
Return swiftly to your original master.
Nine pillars, three beams,
Return to your original place.
The essence of the Five Earths,
The earth qi dissipates and vanishes.
Six Jia, Six Yi,
Disperse the earth swiftly.
Six Bing, Six Ding,
The earth’s dispersal ceases.
Six Wu, Six Ji,
By edict, the earth swiftly rises.
Six Geng, Six Xin,
Suppress the earth without wrath.
Six Ren, Six Gui,
The earth resolves and conceals itself.
Earth Lords, Earth Mothers,
A hundred specters, a thousand spirits.
I know your names,
Today I admonish you.
All gods heed my words,
Vast and majestic.
Heaven is round, Earth is square,
Heaven has nine pillars, Earth has nine beams.
Suppress and disperse all,
Each belongs to the Four Directions.
Guard and protect the gates and doors,
Forever securing auspicious prosperity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Prolonging Life and Delivering from Distress Incantation**
Prolonging life, delivering from distress,
Commanding the divine spirits.
Diminishing calamities for our benefit,

Dispersing misfortune, supporting the weak,
Illuminating my form in reflection.
The talismans inscribed in penetrating oversight,
Align with the divine talismans.
Anciently governing the Seven Origins,
Commanding the Eight Darknesses.
Above, they guard the spirits,
Below, they protect the soul and essence.
In unison with Heaven’s eternal brightness,
Pervading Earth without collapse.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**The Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper**

**Breaking Open Hell’s Prisons**
Vast and boundless, within Fengdu’s depths,
Layer upon layer, the Vajra Mountains stand.
The Limitless Light of the Numinous Treasure,
Illuminates the scorching pools of suffering.
The seven generations of ancestors and all imprisoned souls,
Their forms follow the fragrant clouds and banners.
With the Samadhi Wisdom Blue Lotus,
Ascend to the divine, eternally at peace.

**Sweet Dew Dharma Food Mantra**
Alas for those who suffer in the long night,
Tormented by heat and affliction along the Three Paths.
Fire enters the throat,
Ever tormented by hunger and thirst.
One sprinkle of the Sweet Dew rain,
And the scorching finds cool relief.
The divine souls ascend to the Great Canopy,
Nourishing all beings.

**Dharma Food Rebirth Mantra**
The merit of golden radiance,
Faintly parts the dark and hidden.
The Flower Pool flows with true fragrance,
The lotus canopy follows the drifting clouds.
The immortals, doubly harmonized with the Primordial,
Dwell always within the Twelve Towers.
Swiftly proclaim the Numinous Treasure’s decree,
Roam freely in the celestial paradise.

**Three Lights Flowing Essence Dharma Food Mantra**
The wondrous Dao gives birth to the One Qi,
Within the Qi, yin and yang divide.
Condensing the essence of sun and moon,
Gathered, they flow as the Three Lights.
The Nine Flowers merge with the Nine Paths,
The Eight Colors illuminate the Eight Directions.
Resplendent, they stir the true body,
Flowing essence returns to the Great Vastness.
Below, they descend to the Abyssal Spring Palace,
Above, they array in the Realm of Non-Being.
Bodies unfettered, traces take flight,
Suddenly, all is forgotten.
The Seven Treasures flow with pure essence,
Chaotic and mingled within the Flower Chambers.
Swallowing the Five Rosy Mists,
Peace and harmony endure without end.

**Jade Purity Sweet Dew Dharma Food Mantra**
I bow my head to the Round Net,
Embracing the radiant spirit with luminous form.
Restraining the hun-soul, governing the seven po,
Contemplating and settling at the center.
Walking and sitting, I venerate the Void,
Resting and sleeping, I repose in the Mysterious Chamber.
Hungry, I feast on the yellow sprouts of grain,
Thirsty, I drink the nectar of jade roots.
The divine essence commands the great demons,
Uniting the body to refine the true light.
Reflecting again upon the Great Non-Being,
Ever roaming the empty void.
Perfect interpenetration, waves vanish in deliverance,
True transformation knows no bounds.
Vast and boundless, without end or beginning,
The practitioner must clearly understand.
Silent and serene, forgetting doctrines and teachings,
Responding to the times, unfolding the grand principles.
Descending Dao does not illuminate itself,
One must first enact what is to be done.
Converging in the non-dual realm,
Following the heart, naturally uniting and parting.

**Five Kitchens Spirit Mantra**
One Qi harmonizes with the Great Harmony,
Attaining the One, the Dao is at peace.
Harmony is not one harmony,
The mysterious principle shares the mysterious boundary.
Do not think with thoughts,
Nor seek the thoughtless with thought.
Thinking without thought,
This is the Dharma to be upheld thus.
Do not bind the heart to the heart,
Nor dwell in absolute severance.
With heart present, do not preserve the heart,
In truth, guard the true abyss.
Cultivating principle, abandon the will,
Accumulating cultivation does not depart from it.
With will, do not cultivate the will,
The karma of the past is already known.
All foods gather qi, not all long-stabilized qi gathers.
Qi returns to the original qi,
Take as needed, release as needed.

**Bathing Mantra**
The Divine Water of the Great Mystery,
The origin of the Five Phases.
Born to bathe beings,
Washing away the old, renewing the new.
Thirsty, drink to nourish life,
A rare encounter amidst death and suffering.
Were it not for great compassion,
How could salvation be possible?
Purify the decayed bones,
May they ascend the immortal path.

**Bathing and Changing Clothes Mantra**
The Five Turbidities are now clear,
The Eight Effulgences are now bright.
Today, receiving refinement,
Sins extinguished, blessings born.
Clothing, kerchief, shoes, and sandals,
Adorn the form and appearance.
Now garbed and sashed,
Together ascend the Upper Clarity.

**Summoning the Moon Comet Vermilion Heavenly Lord Mantra**
Essence of utmost yin,
Born of metal and wood.
By the Jade Pivot’s command,
The Thunder Lord of the Great One.
Naked and hair unbound,
Roaming the Three Realms.
Wielding the precious sword,
Drawing lightning, flowing metal.
Thunder listens to the command,
Dispatching the myriad spirits.
One stroke of the divine sword,
Evil spirits vanish in form.
*Oṃ hūṃ hūṃ*, reverently invoking the Nine Heavens’ Flying Stem,
Seizing demons with thunderous roars,
Drawing lightning, the Great One,
The Moon Comet Thunder Lord,
Yang thunder swiftly descends,
Yin thunder swiftly ascends.
Summon the flashing thunder’s light,
Call forth the crashing thunder’s roar.
Reverently summoning the Yang Thunder Messengers: Ma, Guo, Fang, Deng, Tian,
The Yin Thunder Messengers: Zhang, Xu, Yao, Lei, Nan,
Rescue must come first.
Receive the talisman, swiftly arrive,
Slaying and vanquishing must be fierce.
Above and below must connect,
Evil spirits swiftly pursued.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Commanding Thunder to Bring Rain Mantra**
Wind arises from the Xun Gate,
Thunder shakes the Nine Heavens.
Clouds drift through the Azure Vault,
Rain descends before the eaves.
Lightning flashes brilliantly,
Aiding the Dao, connecting with immortals.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Returning the Spirits Mantra**
The master transmits the Upper Dao,
Reverently receiving the decree of the Supreme Mystery.
The commands are now complete,
Driving away and extinguishing the sources of evil.
Return to the original abode,
Lest there be delay.
When later summoned, return again,
Issuing the commands of the Mysterious Origin.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Dispatching Spirits Mantra**
The Five Directions, the Five Mandates,
Heaven yang, earth yin.
Qi follows heaven and earth,
Moving with the divine power of Zhen.
The Five Talismans, the original mandates,
[...] Stem [...] Stars.
Following heaven, enacting the Dao,
Manifesting in the distant and hidden.
Swiftly gather the true qi,
Station and spread the wind and clouds.
Await my commands,
The Five Thunders advance before me.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Thunder Decree**
Thunder’s light, thunder’s light,
The Great One lies concealed.
The command of the Great Earl of Wind,
The Four-Eyed Venerable Elder.
The Emperor Lord guards the waters,
Hurling the fiery essence of yang.
The Rain Master opens,
The Wind Master levels.
Divine might of the moon’s radiance,
The Golden Immortal sets forth.
Water and fire circulate,
Han Bo carries the boat.
The Three Officials open the light,
The Five Emperors trust the hidden.
By the decree of the Supreme,
Dragons fly, rain drips.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Raising Thunder Mantra**
Thunder and lightning pursue each other,
Heaven and earth serve as eyes.
The upright qi of the Eight Directions,
Lightning flashes brilliantly.
Thunder-raising messengers,
Rouse my altar’s bounds,
With crashing thunder and lightning.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Thunderbolt Talisman Mantra**
Essence of Horn and Winnowing Basket,
Divine spirits of Jia and Yi.
Waves surge, drums dance,
Clouds and thunder swiftly arise.

Radiant spirits of Bing and Ding.

Flames follow smoke’s birth.

Swords and halberds cross in array.
Essence of Dipper and Wall,
Stellar spirits of Ren and Gui.
Waves surge, breakers crash,
Guard and protect the afflicted.
Spirits of heaven’s essence,
Heroes of water and fire.
Thunderbolt messengers,
Fire-Bell Generals.
Heavenly Force Officers,
Ten Poles August Lords.
Thunder and fire swiftly rise,
Lightning and hail swiftly race.
Flying frost, battle-axes,
Banners and weapons in profusion.
Wicked gods, demonic ghosts,
Evil specters, malevolent spirits.
Greedily seeking bloody offerings,
Cruelly harming living beings.

Dissolve beneath thunder’s might.
Thousands upon thousands—heads severed,
Myriads upon myriads—forms destroyed.
Those who obey me live,
Those who defy me perish.
Slightest disobedience to my command,
Is rebellion against Supreme Clarity.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Prayer for Clear Skies: Wooden Youth Mantra**

Governing generals and officers, aiding all spirits.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Wooden Youth Mantra II**

Roll back clouds, withdraw rain—now is the hour.

Quickly cease the ceaseless rain—none may disobey.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Oath Mantra of Sudden Fire**
Mighty gods of statutes, Perfected One embracing truth,
Five chariots, eight horses—thunder topples all.
The Supreme Emperor decrees, aiding my divine body.
Threatening light, lightning—reveal your true form at once!
Dare you defy or slight me? You betray the primal covenant.
If I betray you, may I never prosper.
*Oṃ hūṃ hūṃ ūṃ yào xū □ chuǎng □ huǒ □ □ dīng lú □ □ seize the thunder gods.*
*Oṃ hūṃ □ tí ní □ □ zhà hūṃ □ mó tuó zhà yē hūṃ.*
*Oṃ jī hān □ bǔ □ □ jī □ hūṃ □.*

Heavenly thunder, earthly thunder—roar through the eight directions.

Thunder Lords and Mother, Wind Earls and Rain Masters—

Aid me in beheading demons, exterminating evil traitors,
Clearing skies, praying for rain, rescuing the dying, delivering the living.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Oath Chapter of a Hundred Transformations**
Fierce officers of the Three Realms, great gods of sudden fire,
Generals who governed and protected the world under the Yellow Emperor.

On the fifth month’s *wumu* day, ascend into the Southern Palace.
Lord of the Fire Mandate, transforming Heaven and Earth.
Great thunderclaps shake, sudden fire ascends.
Riding dragons through mist, clad in the Yellow Spirit’s vesture.
*Wu* and *Ji* patrol, *Bing* and *Ding* roam.
Pure tea and clear water, a single stick of peach incense burns.
Inscribe my true image, record my true form.
Proclaim my mysterious transformation—I descend at once.
Commanding the Thunder Bureau, fire chariots, fire bells.
Fire-headed warriors, Six Jias and Six Dings.
Abyssal Black Fiends, thunder generals and soldiers.
Patrolling the Three Realms, rising and descending at my behest.
Heaven’s rivers dry, seas boil, molten metal flows.
Fiery chariots strike, great thunder roars.
Breaking caves, smashing temples, beheading demons, annihilating spirits.
Pursuing souls, seizing spirits, manifesting awe-inspiring power.
Wielding axes and drills, iron-faced with bronze eyes.
Dissolving grievances, untying knots, breaking curses, dispelling defilement.
Driving away plagues, severing epidemics, cutting down demonic essences.
Rescuing the people’s suffering, healing the sick and afflicted.
Reviving livelihoods, flourishing all affairs.
Align with my creation—Jade Emperor records my name.
In the Three Palaces and Five Bureaus, ranked among the exalted perfected.
At my left and right, attendants guard and welcome.
Whoever falsely invokes my oath shall be consumed by thunderfire.
Whoever betrays my oath shall be bound by Heaven’s decree.
Wind blades scourge the body, the Six Heavens sever the form.
Swear before Heaven, blood-sealed—never forget this covenant.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Oath of Universal Salvation**
Thunder’s fierce general, sudden fire spirit,
Serving as general in the time of the Yellow Emperor.
Slain in battle against Chiyou, meriting great deeds,
The Jade Emperor decreed him master of thunder.
Wings aflame, soaring with erupting fire,
Teeth like swords, scorching and burning.
Eyes blazing, illuminating Heaven and Earth,
One rage sets seas boiling, mountains collapsing.
Fire chariots and thunderbolts strike the rebellious,
Wood and stone reduced to powder, iron to dust.
Smashing nests, crushing lairs, striking demons,
Burning halls, destroying temples, beheading evil spirits.
Consumption, lingering corpses, and old *qi*,
Plagues and pestilence—all are dispelled.
Untying grievances, releasing entanglements, no lingering attachments,
Averting lawsuits, dispersing disputes, delivering from misfortune.
Inscribe my true image, proclaim my name,
Burn my talismans, manifest my form.
Respond to my call without hindrance—
Be at ease, do not tremble or fear.
Vowing to save the people from all calamities,
Transforming through the Three Realms to aid living beings.
Evil ghosts and treacherous spirits dare not interfere—
One glare of my eyes topples ten thousand evils.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Universal Salvation Incantation**
Fierce officers of thunder, great gods of sudden fire,
Thunder Lords and Lightning Mothers, Wind Earls and Rain Masters.
Marshal Shaoyang, Iron-Faced General,
Envoys of the Five Directions’ barbaric thunder—heed my command!
I have long borne the Dao’s decree, wielding the Emperor’s talisman,
Charged with thunder’s office, solely responsible for execution.
You obey my orders, assisting me.
In beheading demons, driving away plagues,
Severing lingering illnesses, dissolving grievances and knots,
Delivering from calamity, dispelling misfortune,
Breaking shackles, unlocking chains,
Drowning malevolent ghosts, freeing from prisons,
Destroying temples, burning halls,
Sealing mountains, breaking caves,
Seizing ghosts, pursuing souls, rescuing the people’s suffering.
For all prayers and supplications, you must exert yourselves.
Wind and fire unceasing, clearly manifesting your duties.
Carefully abiding by the mysterious covenant, oaths blood-sealed.
By the Jade Emperor’s decree, never dare disobey.
Go swiftly, come swiftly, grandly display thunder’s might.
I stand before the altar, sword drawn, awaiting swift response.

Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Central Heaven Swift-Fire Statute Deity**
Spread *qi*, march gods, raise thunder, ignite fire,
Wield clouds, unleash fierce smoke, hurl lightning and hail,
Thunderous roars shake.
Zhen Palace’s Year Star raises thunder; Li Palace’s Fire Star ignites flame.
Tai Bai Star rises from clouded Kan Palace; Chen Star brings rain from the center.
Zhen Star commands wind, sweeping away all inauspicious omens.
Wherever I walk or sit, the Great One and Moon Comet Star Lords
March thunder, deploy lightning, exterminate demonic vapors,
Subdue lingering *qi* of the dead, and dispel all misfortune.

Heavenly fire, earthly fire, Samadhi true fire—
A single flash summons the Five Thunders, stars march and thunder rises.
Fire gods Wen, Zhao, Zhu, and Ma Chen
Execute lawless spirits, regardless of rank—ghosts obliterated by thunder and lightning.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Subduing Demons Incantation**
From the Primordial arises life, the Five Thunders’ mighty gods.
Opening heaven, cleaving earth, subduing fierce stars.
Ten thousand legions of fierce fire, a thousand hosts of yakshas.
Four heads, eight arms, gaping maws, golden eyes.
Towering ten thousand *zhang*, devouring demons and consuming spirits.
Breathing wind and rain, roaring thunder.
Thunder Lords hurl thunderbolts, Lightning Mothers pour molten metal.
Wind and thunder drum, heaven and earth darken.
Slaying dragons, beheading monsters, sun and moon stand still.
Heavenly gods bow in submission, earthly deities welcome.
Nine Heavens’ Qian trigram, sun, moon, and stars—
Flying Heavenly Divine Kings, each and all heed.
Nine Earths’ Kun trigram, springs, depths, and underworld.
Northern Capital of Fengdu, abyssal Four Seas.
Earth officials, water bureaus, scrutinizing ghostly camps.
Ever walking the true Dao, nurturing all beings.
Dare any transgress, harming living souls—
Summoned by talismanic command, thunder and lightning execute.
Beheaded, burned, reduced to dust.
Might unopposable, guilt inescapable.
Saving people, aiding the world, ranked among the Nine Heavens.
Hymns sung by all heavens, divine merit ascends daily.
Commanding the Three Realms, enslaving the ten thousand spirits.
Beheading demons, slaying monsters, thunder and lightning fly.
Baluo’s mighty clouds, Danli’s radiant glow.
Aqu’s vast expanse, Bi’s scarlet-robed gaze.
Drums resound with subtle wonders, Nanlu hurls fire.
Fuyan’s stone oath, Jiyan’s Dipper clash.
Xuyan, Fire Lord, Anu speaks above.
Drums and Harmonious Mother, Shen Zhu and Awu attend.
Lunfu’s bright longevity, Kui and Bi’s far-reaching plans.
Fortune’s hymns, true and unchanging, thunder’s hidden mysteries.
Recite ten thousand times, in harmony with the divine.
Unite sun and moon, divine power fully arrayed.
Ren, Gui, Zi, and Hai—recite this scripture.
True spirits guard and protect, in unity with the Dao.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Breaking Demons Incantation**
Nine Heavens’ nine *qi*, a million heavenly soldiers.
Above, they govern heavenly demons; below, they inspect the underworld.
A thousand gods bow in submission, ten thousand demons assume form.
Devouring stars and moon, lords of the Three Realms.
Mouths spewing fierce fire, molten metal and fire bells.
Thunder, wind, lightning, rain, blades and swords in profusion.
Divine power guards and shields, homes flourish and prosper.
Demons dare not trespass, ghosts and spirits vanish.
Plagues and pestilence flee, altars purified and solemn.
Five Thunder Divine Generals pacify and guard households.
By Jade Emperor’s decree, no mercy is granted.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Gathering Incantation**
Yin spirits, yin spirits—heaven trembles, earth darkens.

Those who resist thunder perish; those who follow thrive.

Expelling evil, beheading demons, protecting all beings.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Incantation for Resolving Karmic Entanglements**
Heaven resolves, Earth resolves; Yin resolves, Yang resolves.
Obstinate attachments of past-life parents, resolve.
Seven generations of ancestors, eight generations of vengeful foes—curses and entanglements, resolve.
Present-life parents and in-laws—curses and entanglements, resolve.
Debtors, resolve. Those owed, resolve.
Mandarin-duck vows, secret trysts, resentful longings, resolve.
Before the hearth, behind the stove; before the gods, at the Buddha’s abode—grievances born in life, complaints voiced in death, self-made vows and self-sworn oaths—all curses and vows, resolve.
Mountain caves and grotto palaces—lewd spirits, malevolent ghosts, demonic pregnancies, resolve.
Blood Lakes and Gorge Rocks; Thirty-Six Bureaus, Seventy-Two Clerks—karmic entanglements and obstinate grievances from kalpas past, resolve.
Resolved or unresolved, all must swiftly resolve, swiftly resolve.
Should you fail to resolve, delay even a moment, defy the command or violate the talisman—iron-faced Thunder Gods will show no mercy.
Eradicate your haunting form, extinguish your haunting essence.
Thunder’s axe shall cleave you into dust, ground to powder.
Swiftly, swiftly, as decreed by statute and command.

**Five-Thunder Summoning Incantation for Hastening Birth**

The Three Realms obey the command,
sun and moon revolve like jade disks.
Mists and vapors surge,
rivers and seas roar.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands!

**Summoning of Generals and Marshals**
I summon the generals and marshals—hasten to descend!
Come to the altar and heed my command,
to execute and slay demonic spirits.
Mountain specters and goblins,
reduced to fine dust.
Move mountains, topple peaks—
primordial, prosperous, harmonious, steadfast.
Fire-Wheel Divine Generals, delay not!
Where the talisman’s command arrives,
swiftly obey!
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands!

**Summoning of the Merit-Officer Incantation**

swiftly manifest divine radiance!
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands!

**Summoning of the Metal-Fire Heavenly Soldiers Incantation**

Hasten from the Xun Palace, descend to the Li Gate.

The heart as general, *qi* as the spirit.
I now merge and unite,
condensing into form.
Ingested, it becomes the elixir;
exhaled, it becomes the spirit.
Heaven and Earth conjoin in virtue,
sun and moon conceal their radiance.
Hasten to descend,
and merge with my true essence!
Swiftly, swiftly, as the law commands!

**Fire Enclosure Incantation**
Source of the sun, ancestor of fire, essence of the Vermilion Numinous Fire Prefecture.
Fire Bell deities, Fire Wheel deities, Fire deities enclose the spirits.
Form a net to capture malevolent essences, the Fire Enclosure spans the eight directions.
The world flames with fire, transmuting into an iron net.
Fire Officials, Fire Lords, Fire Emperors, Fire deities—
regardless of rank, all malevolent spirits causing harm,
enclose them all, hunt down and seize the malevolent essences.
As I enact the Fire Enclosure,
above it pierces the Azure Clouds’ boundless heavens,
below it reaches the Dharma Realm of the Wind Wheel.
Eastward to the Land of Wood’s Origin,
westward to the Heaven of Metal’s Ancestor,
southward to the Vermilion Numinous Prefecture,
northward to the Great Luo Heaven.
Above, spirits may not descend;
below, spirits may not ascend.
Within, spirits may not escape;
without, spirits may not enter.
What spirit is not within my enclosure?
What spirit is not within my cavern?
I reverently summon the Great Fire Enclosure deities Xu Zhong, Jiang Ju, Zhao Yu, and Zhai Ning,
to receive my decree and heed my command,
execute with utmost haste!

**Black Enclosure Incantation**
The Four Heavens sealed, black clouds shroud the eight directions.
Above, they reach the Black Marsh of the Celestial River;
below, they descend to the Ninefold Dark Yin.
Black winds howl, black mists surge.
Black nets, black webs, black ropes, black wheels.
Black thunder, black hail, black *qi* clouds.
As I enact the Black Enclosure, it binds the ghostly souls.
Malevolence grieves, specters wail, spirits weep.
I reverently summon:
Marshal Tianpeng, Commander of the Hosts;

Manifesting transformations, displaying divine might.
Regardless of rank,
whether kin or stranger,
Golden Immortals or Ancient Buddhas—
erase their traces, obliterate their forms.
For those who practice malevolent rites,
sever them without pause.
Tear up bricks, hurl tiles,
fling stones, raise dust.
Mountains crumble, seas dry,
fire extinguished, earth leveled.
All are seized, nowhere to flee.
The human realm shines bright,
the ghostly gate is pitch-black.
The Great Dao flourishes,
the Immortal Dao prospers.
The Demon Dao vanishes,
the Ghost Dao leaves no trace.
Seen yet unseen,
heard yet unheard.
A thousand leagues of darkness,
ten thousand miles of gloom.
Heaven black, earth black,
the Yellow River black,
heaven and earth, mountains and rivers—
inky black.
Vastly spread the all-encompassing enclosure,
to enclose the spirits and souls for me.
Hasten, lead the troops to the eight extremities,
capture them alive and bring them to the altar court.
By the decree of the Supreme Purple Tenuity Emperor,
I enact the Great Black Enclosure to capture all.
