**Hundun (Primordial Chaos) Dharma Incantation**
I am the primordial yang spirit of the Golden Gates,
born of the undifferentiated *qi* of Hundun.
Heaven revolves, earth rotates, the cosmos turns—
the Primordial Ancestor aids me in summoning the stellar perfected.
Iron master, golden sword, dispel demonic miasma,
command thunder, dispatch lightning, resound in the Great Clarity.
Dare any arrive late, their forms shall be destroyed first.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

Disheveled, I pace the stem steps to seek baleful *qi*,
sword tip ignites fire to refine the true script.
The Old Lord bestowed upon me the Hundun Dharma,
to command the stellar perfected and the Six Dings.
One *qi* circulates seven times—heaven and earth darken,
at the third watch’s third point, summon the thunder gods.
Only the summoning thunder’s linchpin,
a profoundly arcane formula few know.
Poria-cooked porridge refines the stellar perfected,
ever retaining a single point to summon the thunder gods.
For one *shi* and eight *ke*, fire follows the body,
spirit talismans align with the celestial apertures.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

The marrow of heaven and earth,
the essence of yin and yang.
*Qian* revolves, *kun* turns,
the linchpin summons the stellar perfected.
The eleven luminaries,
co-regents with the Emperor.
Hundun vast and boundless,
the primordial *qi* first divides.
Heaven opens, earth stands,
seizing ghosts, driving spirits.
Giving rise to the ten thousand kinds,
nurturing the host of numina.
The Hundun Dharma’s laws,
all gods heed without fail.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Hundun Talismanic Decree**
I act on behalf of the Most High Lord Lao,
the Heavenly Worthy above the Nine Heavens,
the thirty-two heavens as my crown,
the thirty-two heavens as my body.
I enact the great Hundun Dharma,
commanding all suns, moons, and stars.
Myriad sages heed my dispatch,
thousand perfected guard the altar’s gate.
Before mountains, rivers, and the Five Peaks existed,
there was the Primordial Lord of the Mysterious Origin.
I bear the Primordial Ancestor’s decree,
to behead ghosts, slay demons, annihilate spirits.
Should any defy my laws,
their heads and forms shall be severed, rootless.
For the state, swiftly bring rain;
for the people, swiftly seize ghosts.
Should any thunder gods disobey,
punish them to become the underworld’s yin soldiers.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Decree of Dispatch**
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

The emerald waters ripple with autumn’s crystalline clarity,
A thousand-catty iron axe rests lightly on my shoulder.
By the river, willows sway and topple in the wind—
Even if I held Chang’e in my arms, I would not flinch.

Light as dust drifting in the void,
Heavy as iron weighed by a thousand steelyards.
White as snow descending from the heavens,
Red as the blood of the crimson ape.

Weaver Girl’s Fourth Brother darkens the earth below,
Goulou Jili veils the moon in cloud.
The monk ascends, bathed in the glow of the new night’s moon,
Great Simplicity and Primordial Dawn dwell in the Water-Fire Cavern.
Kunlun’s completion fills the mountains and rivers—
At this moment, heaven and earth dare not speak.

I command the heavens, I command the earth, I command the clouds and thunder,
Exhausting the numinous talismans to summon the Nine Capitals.
Should one master the art of commanding the heavens,
They may enlist the Nine Celestial Lords of the Southern Bureau.
Cloud-dragons coil and coil, dispatching the Five Thunders,
Feng Yi dances and chews the Nine Dragons.

Vast and boundless, filling the cosmos,
The sun and moon shift, mountains and peaks obey.
Lightning flashes, thunder cracks like a whip,
Shattering rocks, bursting springs, overturning mountains and seas.
Waters roar, dragons howl, flying stones shriek,
Mountains collapse, boulders split, the earth’s decrees crumble.

City gods who defy my commands shall be beheaded in the thoroughfare,
The Three Thousand Worlds shall be overturned again and again.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Incantation for Refining the Body**
Heaven and earth transform into qi,
Yin unites with yang’s spirit.
Upper qi descends,
The two qi intertwine and surge.
As the upper descends, the lower resounds—
Thunder’s voice erupts.
The Three-Five Thunder Gods,
Generals of slaughter and conquest.
The thunder’s voice transforms all—
*Primal, prosperous, steadfast, and upright.*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Incantation for Transforming the Spirit**
The Primordial Heavenly Worthy,
One qi divides into the true.
Poured into my body,
It transforms my true form.
Riding the wind, harnessing qi,
A body beyond the body.
Just as the Scenic Empyrean’s
Protector Hua, the Perfected.
The Four Beasts encircle without,
The stars and constellations descend above.
Thunder gods obey the command,
Crushing and shearing demonic hordes.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Incantation for the Five Kalpas Unfolding the Chart**
The Dragon Han unfolds the chart,
Responding to nature’s transformations.
The Crimson Brightness inaugurates the era,
Brahma’s practice spans the Nine Heavens.
The August One manifests numinous signs,
Wondrously resonating with the Celestial Origin.
The Yan Kang floats in ethereal clarity,
Soaring to the Great Mystery.
The Kai Huang kalpa cycles,
Myriad qi unite as immortals.
Cinnabar radiance dawns,
Molten metal subdues demons.
The Luminous Numinous returns to the path,
The Cinnabar Grove harnesses the whirlwind.
The Azure Numinous gathers the true,
Receiving the mandate of the Divine Empyrean.
The Primordial Numinous seizes qi,
The Mystic Mist pervades the void.
The Five Numinous dissolve demons,
Flowing fire forms the crested plume.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Scenic Empyrean Talisman Incantation**
The Scenic Empyrean issues its decree,
The talisman summons the thunder gods.
The Lunar Generals transmit the call,
Hastening through the clouds in urgency.
Conveying through the Three Realms,
Swiftly reaching the Xun City.
Subtle and obscure, veiled in purity,
The Jade Principle’s distant peace—
The master’s summons grows ever stronger.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Scenic Empyrean Thunder Incantation**
The Scenic Empyrean governs the central pole,
Harnessing qi to soar with the immortals.
Whirling steps upon the wind’s net,
The Azure Lads ascend the empyrean.
Numinous illumination hastens the divine,
Reflected light ascends the Grand Tenuity.
The Five Thunders swiftly descend,
Merging in accord with the mysterious mechanism.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Incantation for Summoning the Scenic Empyrean’s Direct Talisman**
The flying talisman moves with swift urgency,
Aiding the mandate of the Nine Empyreans.
Roaming the great void,
Rushing clouds, calling winds.
Transmit the command above,
The Divine Emperor’s decree.
You summon thunder and lightning,
Your rhythm matches the numinous radiance.
Ascend with solemn majesty,
The Three Realms swiftly descend.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Lunar General Incantation**
Heaven is clear, earth is tranquil,
Yin and yang intertwine.
Hear my single summons—
Hasten to descend.
[Specific] Lunar General,
Swiftly appear before the altar.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Scenic Empyrean Dipper Qi Incantation**
Seated to guard the Celestial Dipper,
Following the Dipper’s four directions.
In spring, dwell in the Zhen position,
In summer, occupy the Fire quadrant.
In autumn, approach the Dui position,
In winter, reside in the Zi region.
Ancestral qi gives rise to the four seasons,
Auxiliary qi follows the Dipper’s path.
The Dipper turns with the seasons,
Qi revolves around the Ladle and Dipper.
Facing is yin,
Turning away is yang.
Jia, Geng, Ding, Gui—
The chosen hour is auspicious.
At the winter and summer solstices,
Draw qi from the Dipper’s edge.
The method for drawing qi:
Face the direction and sit.
Eyes dark yet red,
The two qi soar.
Descending from heaven,
Merging with my true light.
Receive it at the crown,
Qi pours into the distant radiance.
The crown senses the qi’s chisel,
Like fire scorching boiling water.
The skull opens of itself,
Passing through the gates and barriers.
No obstruction, no hindrance—
Attain the audience with the Primordial King.
The Dipper divides into six colors,
Separating yin and yang.
Sealing the decree, stabilizing qi,
Repelling ghosts with the Slaying Dipper.
Nurturing the body’s generative qi,
Protecting the embryo with the Prosperous Dipper.
Yang qi governs yin,
Yin qi governs yang.
Those who can gather them
Become the Dharma Kings.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Golden Light Decree**
The Jade Emperor’s few decrees,
Disseminate the Dharma to the host of perfected.
Above the Nine Heavens,
Five-colored auspicious clouds.
Golden light intertwines,
Illuminating the cosmos.
Repelling demons, annihilating specters,
Commanding and restraining the myriad spirits.
The Xun gate swiftly shatters,
Thunderously obliterating malevolent essences.
The Three Realms heed the command,
The Nine Bureaus take heed.
*Primal, prosperous, steadfast, and upright—*
Swiftly manifest your true form!
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Incantation for Commanding the Spirits**
Command my body,
Command my spirit.
I am the Jade Tenuity’s Preceptor and Minister,
Leading the ten thousand troops of the Mysterious Heaven.
A colossal rainbow lion follows the thunder,
Heaven’s gates and earth’s axes shrouded in black clouds.
The Eight Slayers and Six Dings hurl fire bells,
Roaming the Three Realms to capture demonic essences.
Those who dare arrive late shall be the first to perish in form and spirit.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

To my left, the Sun Lord,
To my right, the Moon Lord.
Before me, thunder and lightning,
Behind me, wind and clouds.
Hear my commands,
Receive my instructions.
Shaking heaven and earth in wrath,
The Twelve Generals.
Each arrays their ranks,
Swiftly descending with majestic power.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

**Incantation for Subduing Demons**
Great Thunder Lord of the Universe,
Thunderbolts fill the empty sky.
Three hundred thousand blades and soldiers,
Slaying *qi* to guard heaven and earth.

Seizing lightning to shatter the wicked.
Iron-faced, capturing demons,

All ghosts vanish without a trace.
Decrees resound with celestial authority,

Should any refuse to submit,
The law shall brook no tolerance.
From the Dipper’s bowl to its handle,
To the depths of the Nine Springs.
Great thunder and fire of the universe,
Subdue all into pure and tranquil wind.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as the law decrees!*

For ten thousand kalpas without end.

The Great Sun reveals its true Wheel of Fire,

Dare to defy or slight—punishment shall not be light!
Water Department’s Judges, hasten to comply.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in law and decree!*

**Rain-Cessation Prayer**
August Heaven suddenly decrees no delay,
The Water Department obeys—dragon spirits take alarm.
Gathering clouds disperse, mists scatter, the Four Heavens clear.
Fierce winds blow, yin dissolves and does not congeal.
The Great Sun’s radiance shines, solar qi brightens.
With the talisman, rain halts, skies open to clarity.
*Oṃ! Fire Wheel, Wind Wheel, swiftly seize!*
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in law and decree!*

**Luminous Yin’s Auspicious Prayer**

Pure Yang remains unwaning.

**Vast Fortune Prayer**

With celestial divine qi,
Attack the ghostly qi below earth.

All shall be expelled.
Immediately, both exterior and interior shall be activated:
If sweat is present, attack the sweat, causing it to break and disperse.
If phlegm is present, attack the phlegm, causing it to be vomited.
If perversity is present, attack and expel it, causing it to submit.
Treat according to the symptoms.
*Swiftly, swiftly, as in law and decree!*

**Scripture of the Supreme Three Caverns’ Divine Incantations, Scroll Twelve**
**Miscellaneous Incantations for Leisurely Retreats, Prayers, and Purifications**
**Five Directions’ Guardian Spirit Incantation**

Nine Qi Azure Heavens, Radiant Star Great Spirit.
Shining upon the eastern quarter, penetrating the Nine Gates.
Revolving candle of yang light, sweeping away filth and dispelling miasma.
Luminous Youth, named Mystic Quarter.
Guarding my chamber, facing the Imperial Lord above.
Seizing demons and binding specters, hunting down malevolent hordes.
Upholding the true Dao, vermilion script on jade.
Nine Heavens’ talismanic command, transmitted by dragon couriers.
All under heaven pacified and secured, I attain transcendence as a flying immortal.

**Northeastern Mighty Spirit,**
Vast and boundless as Zhanglong,
Clad in white, wielding the sword, sweeping away demonic sects.
Wherever the heavenly might points, a hundred suppressions leave no trace.
The Six Harmonies are serene and prosperous, greatly aiding the divine work.

**Southeastern Mighty Spirit,**
Fiery flames and scorching winds,
Clad in azure, wielding the sword, dispelling demonic calamities.
Earth spirits and spectral suppressions are captured and sent to the Demon-Quelling Star.
The numinous altar is solemn and pure, the celestial radiance shines brilliantly.

**Southwestern Mighty Spirit,**
Dissolving filth in Qianliang,
Clad in black, wielding the sword, driving and executing demonic [omission].
The five earths extinguish suppressions, forever severing inauspiciousness.
Heaven and earth are pure and tranquil, the myriad Brahma realms unfold.

**Northwestern Mighty Spirit,**
Solemn and still in Fangyang,
Clad in white, wielding the sword, grasping the celestial writ.
Prostrate corpses and venomous suppressions keep far from the altar precinct.
They may not linger—heavenly statutes crush and harm.

Lush and verdant, the azure essence—
The radiant scene opens in clarity.
At the inception of yang, the nine qi bloom, nurturing the soul.
Flowing blossoms in the wondrous treasury, the numinous and true Upper Spirits,
Adorned with jade and azure cloud crowns, flying light upon feathered skirts.
Azure-waisted Jade Maidens, the Supreme Perfected,
Preserve and convey the immortal registers, dispelling demons and repelling miasma.

The Prosperous Yang True Elder, the Venerable Red Spirit,
Commands the Cinnabar Heaven, restraining and binding demonic hordes.
Sternly driving vermilion phoenixes, unicorns with three horns,
Ascending the Great Clarity of the Dao, the root of the Mysterious Origin.
Flaming embers of the three qi coil in crimson clouds,
Nurturing the cinnabar treasury, preserving the kalpa’s long endurance.

The Seven Numinous Radiant Qi, the Three Primal Pure Ones—
Within them abides the August Elder, restraining and seizing demonic essences.
The Generals of the Geng and Xin Palaces, seventy million troops,
With feathered banners and dragon-tasseled staffs, golden tigers and cloud-charging steeds.
Severing delusive specters, refining and nurturing blossoming splendor,
They endure with the Dao through kalpas, unshaken across eons.

The Northern Yin’s gloomy expanse, the Palace of Mysterious Qi,
Where the Imperial Perfected and numinous hosts convene, driving spirits and dragon-chariots.
Within its chambers dwell Jade Maidens and Night-Luminous Lads,
Who grasp and wield the talismanic registers, seizing and subduing demonic traces.
The Void and Danger constellations conjoin in transformation, purple mists stirring winds.
Treasured crystals refine and nurture, transcending the limits of post-celestial time.

The Peerless August Upper Spirit, the Revered One of Primordial Wonder,
Merging and harmonizing with uncarved simplicity, the root of creation’s origin.
Moved by subtle and profound stirrings, great deities spontaneously arise,
Drawing and summoning the ten thousand qi, assembling in the Hall of Splendor.
Dispelling the hundred demons, flourishing together with the Dao,
Preserving and delivering from calamity, dissolving trials and averting misfortune.

**Purification Incantation for Fengdu’s Frigid Court**
The Frigid Court holds much sorrow and suffering;
Turn the heart to worship the Primal August One.
The Nüqing Spirit-Treasure Talisman, the Celestial Emperor’s writ of Zhongshan—
With one recitation, ascend to the Grand Clarity;
With a second, contemplate the Great Vastness.
Merit extends to the Nine Dark Realms,
Spiraling upward to the Purple Void.

**Incantation for Bathing the Deceased**
O majestic and virtuous Honored One,
Your meritorious deeds now perfected and complete.
Descending in body to receive and guide,
The Master’s treasure naturally accompanies.
Compassionately sprinkling the Dharma-water,
To wash away delusion and sinking confusion.
Eternally delivered to the Three Clarities’ shore,
Forever parting from the Five Defilements’ mire.

**Incantation for Transforming Robes**
The Nine Luminaries lend their aid,
True qi transforms the garments.
The four seasons unite in protection,
The five planets interweave their radiance.
Qi divides into silk brocade,
Colors gather to proclaim majesty.
The Six Directions lend their support,
The Three Qi’s subtle mysteries.
The Most Perfected shine resplendently,
Immortal maidens soar in unison.
Cloud-script crowns and sashes,
Solemn and pure, the celestial mechanism.
Round blossoms of pristine clarity,
The Primordial Beginning’s compassion here.

**Incantation for Sweet Dew Dharma-Food**
Cool and flowing, the sweet dew nourishes,
Its Dharma-flavor beyond thought or conjecture.
The fragrance of the Seven Perfected wafts,
In profound obscurity, how could doubt arise?
Those who receive this Dharma-food
Ascend to heaven, enter the Purple Tenuity.
Roaming and feasting in the Great Upper Capital,
Their radiance boundless, without limit.

**Incantation for the Three Lights’ Transformed Food**
Vast essence generates Dharma-qi,
Misty and dense, it congeals in the heavens.
The Two Luminaries together clarify,
The Five Planets intermingle and commune.
The Three Lights blaze resplendently,
Precious qi gathers in the Three Palaces.
The Emperor’s realm convenes the Nine Elders,
Swallowing and imbibing, the hundred bones flourish.
Golden blossoms illuminate the scene,
Body and sun and moon as one.
Recite before the Upper Saints,
Through ten thousand kalpas, life without end.

**Incantation for Universal Salvation Dharma-Food**
The food of the Celestial Kitchen arises naturally,
I now bestow empowerment upon it.
A single grain pervades the ten directions,
As numerous as the Ganges’ sands, all delusions sink.
Hunger and thirst forever vanish,
Feasting in the Jasper Pool.
Now offered to the departed spirits,
Its merit beyond all reckoning.

**Incantation for Jade Yang’s Refined Transformed Food**
The true qi of Jade Yang,
The wondrous Dao divides into Three Luminaries.
In profound harmony, the numinous sound is sung,
The Eight Assemblies spread forth jeweled scriptures.
The Five Elders feast on the Cinnabar Terrace,
Floating, floating, riding the luminous clouds.
The Great Saints and hosts of all heavens,
Turn their chariots to drink the jade nectar.
The Three and Five determine the register of life,
Frolicking as guests of the Most High.
Radiant splendor shines boundlessly,
Hand in hand, they ascend to the Jade Dawn.

**Incantation for Cloud Blossom’s Refined Transformed Food**
Drawing qi beyond the Dark Net,
Nine rays weave into cloud blossoms.
The Seven Dawns’ lofty Dao,
The Three Qi illuminate vermilion clouds.
Offering incense, imbibing the essence of dawn,
Merit fulfilled, the world’s net is undone.
Refining and transforming until the dust-kalpa’s end,
A hundred million kalpas would not be too many.
Dropping one’s name from the Three Realms’ court,
Befriending the Most High’s family.
Riding the luminous chariot, bowing to the Mysterious Dipper,
What need to traverse the Eight Extremities?

**Incantation for Guiding Immortals’ Refined Transformed Food**
The natural and perfect Dao,
Wondrous beyond the profound within the profound.
The ten thousand heavens pay homage at the Jade Steps,
The Five Elders attend the Flowery Canopy.
The Three Lights hold numinous qi,
Only the sagely and worthy are delivered.
Diligently cultivate the immortal’s calling,
Swallowing and rinsing, consuming the blossoming root.
Spirit and form unite with the Three Images,
Vast and distant, returning to the original root.
Phoenixes and crows soar through the Ten Heavens,
Taking flight without a backward glance.

**Incantation for Precious Qi’s Refined Transformed Food**
Far, far above the Three Heavens,
Lofty, lofty, the Nine Dark Terraces.
Golden lads gather the harvest,
Jade maidens return bearing flowers.
The Celestial Guests bow to the immortal visitors,
Rising and descending the Jade Stairs.
The Heavenly River irrigates the Eastern Well,
Precious qi congeals from the void.
Swallowing and rinsing the jeweled nectar,
For a million kalpas, never again to decline.
Raising one’s head toward the Three Clarities’ path,
Brushing one’s robes—what joy!

**Incantation for Fixed Light’s Refined Transformed Food**
The perfect Dao of the Highest Heaven,
Wondrous indeed, the Numinous Treasure’s scriptures.
Inhaling the luminous essence, guiding the Five Stars,
Swallowing and rinsing, preserving the blossoming rays.
Flowing essence irrigates the hundred bodies,
Radiant crystals congeal like frost and snow.
Penetrating and illuminating within and without,
All dust and dross utterly vanish.
The body’s flesh never again ages,
Attaining this, it is called Fixed Light.
Forever feasting in the Hall of Great Clarity,
This is the Land of Unending Day.
Drawing one’s traces back to the root,
Nine transformations congeal true constancy.

**Incantation for Delivering and Rebirth**
Diligently cultivate the Great Dao’s methods,
With focused heart, move the Great Obscurity.
The true qi of Yellow Blossoms descends,
The five viscera knit the fetal infant.
The departed are born in heaven’s halls,
Ascending in flight to pay homage in the Upper Clarity.
Blessings and grace extend without exception.
This food is bestowed upon all beings.

**Talismanic Incantations for Deliverance from Suffering**

**Incantation for the Talisman of Salvation from Suffering**
The Primordial Supreme Sage, the August Jade Emperor,
Jade script proclaims the decree, delivering the dead and rebirthing the living.
Golden Register’s wondrous precepts, rescuing and uplifting the dark netherworld.
White writ of precious script, the Nine Perfected’s mysterious canon.
Dissolving transgressions and debts, settling grievances in peace.
The Perfected of Salvation from Suffering, excising all sins and punishments.
The Attendant of Fate’s Register, inscribes names for rebirth.
Guardian deities of the precepts escort them to the courts of fortune.
Transcending the Five Sufferings, they ride cloud chariots.
Turning the Wheel, they attain the Dao, ascending in flight to the Upper Clarity.

**Incantation for the Talisman of Longevity**
The Most High and Radiant, the Primordial Overseer of the Perfected.
The Five Venerable Lords of Heaven, the vermilion script of jade writ.
Redeeming all, severing the roots of karmic debts.
All receive liberation, tortures and trials cease.
The hun-soul ascends to the Nine Heavens, the po-soul crosses to Crimson Mound.
Today, this proclamation is made—ten thousand spirits heed.
Dragons bear the white writ, sealing the pact with true numina.
As wished, without delay, wind and fire unceasing.

**Incantation for the Golden Writ of Precious Edict**
The Three Heavens’ Great Net, the Most High Jade Clarity.
The Primordial’s numinous script, the Most High’s true writ.
The Great Dao of the Mysterious Origin, descending from the Jade Palace.
The Perfected of the Great Cavern Heaven, governing the divine souls.
The Lords of the Nine Netherworlds, the true numina of the Six Caverns.
Receive the true talisman, deliver the dark souls.
By the decree of the Heavenly Kings, descend swiftly and act.

**Incantation for the True Talisman to Shatter Hell**
The Most Sagely Divine Person, the Most Sincere Perfected.
Descendants of the Primordial August, grandchildren of the Most High.
Countless generations of ancestors, suffering souls of the dark netherworld.
The Heavenly Worthy’s great dharma, ten revolutions to restore the numinous.
Vermilion script forms the chapter, proclaimed to the gates of the underworld.
With one stroke of jade writ, the iron city crumbles.
The talisman’s light blazes, piercing the dense darkness.
Blades transform into jade trees, swords become towering forests.
Flaming fires birth lotuses, ice melts and snowy gates dissolve.
The Three Paths and Five Sufferings, the Eight Difficulties transcended.
Demon kings and nether officials bow in reverence and escort.
By the command of the Upper Clarity, all comply without fail.

**Incantation for the True Talisman of the Verified Register to Break Hell’s Bonds**
In the cold night of the Nine Springs, through kalpas of cyclic suffering,
In the dark abyss of night, suddenly light shines.
Piercing the Nine Ramparts, vajra shatters and crumbles.
Wind and thunder disperse, fiery veils become pools.
The frigid depths warm, all torments cease.
Chariots of fire extinguish their flames, cauldrons cease their boiling.
Bronze pillars collapse, butchery halts.
By the Primordial
